## Turn 1

### User

 Fpos High-Density Specs: Wallet & No-Receipt Returns
Project Scope:

API Types: packages/freshon-api/src/types.ts
POS Store: Fpos/src/pos/store.ts
Checkout: Fpos/src/pos/components/PaymentDrawer.tsx
Returns: Fpos/src/pos/components/ReturnScreen.tsx
 Task 1: Type & Store Infrastructure
1. Update Types (freshon-api/src/types.ts):

Add "Wallet" to PosPaymentMethod.
Add wallet_balance: number to PosCustomer.
2. Update Store Actions (store.ts):

Add fetchCustomerTransactions: (phone: string) => Promise<Transaction[]> action. This should call a backend endpoint that returns orders filtered by the customer's phone number.
Update pay and processRefund to support the "Wallet" method.
 Task 2: Wallet Checkout (PaymentDrawer.tsx)
Requirements:

UI: Add a "WALLET" button in the method selection grid.
Display: Show the customer's current balance next to the button: (Bal: ₹500).
Logic: If the total is greater than customer.wallet_balance, disable the "WALLET" button and show a "Low Wallet Balance" alert.
Priority: Default to Wallet if the customer is a "PRIDE" member and has a balance.
 Task 3: No-Receipt Return Workflow (ReturnScreen.tsx)
Objective: Allow returns even if the customer lost their receipt.

New Workflow:

Search: Add a search bar to find a customer by Phone Number.
History: When a customer is selected, display a list of their Last 5 Transactions (Receipt ID, Date, Amount).
Select: When the operator clicks a transaction, load it into the return view just as if they had scanned a receipt.
Refund Priority: Default the "Refund Method" to "Wallet".
 Task 4: Store Updates (store.ts)
Update the pay function to handle the logic:

If method === "Wallet", ensure the backend transaction is logged as a wallet deduction.
Update local selectedCustomer.wallet_balance after a successful wallet payment or refund.
 Note for Kimi: Use the existing "Sharp/Brutalist" UI components. The transaction list in the return screen should use a simple, high-contrast table format.

   601	  subtotal: number;
   602	  member_discount: number;
   603	  surcharge: number;

   607	}

   111	
   112	export const PRIDE_DISCOUNT_PCT = 0.10;
   113	
   114	// ─── Derived Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   115	
   116	export const memberPriceOf = (
   117	  p: { unitPrice: number; memberEligible?: boolean },
   118	  pride: boolean
   119	) =>
   120	  pride && p.memberEligible
   121	    ? +(p.unitPrice * (1 - PRIDE_DISCOUNT_PCT)).toFixed(2)
   122	    : p.unitPrice;
   123	
   124	export const lineTotal = (i: CartItem, pride: boolean) =>
   125	  memberPriceOf(i, pride) * i.quantity;
   126	
   127	export const subtotalOf = (cart: CartItem[], pride = false) =>
   128	  cart.reduce((s, i) => s + lineTotal(i, pride), 0);
   129	
   130	export const grossSubtotalOf = (cart: CartItem[]) =>
   131	  cart.reduce((s, i) => s + i.unitPrice * i.quantity, 0);
   132	
   133	export const surchargeOf = (subtotal: number, m: PaymentMethod) =>
   134	  m === "Sodexo" ? +(subtotal * 0.05).toFixed(2) : 0;
   135	
   136	export const formatINR = (n: number) =>
   137	  "₹" + n.toLocaleString("en-IN", { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
   138	
   139	// ─── Store Interface ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

   141	interface PosState {
   142	  // Theme
   143	  theme: Theme;
   144	  toggleTheme: () => void;

   240	  clearReturn: () => void;

   242	
   243	// ─── Store Implementation ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   244	
   245	export const usePos = create<PosState>((set, get) => ({
   246	  // Theme
   247	  theme: "dark",
   248	  toggleTheme: () => set((s) => ({ theme: s.theme === "dark" ? "light" : "dark" })),
   249	
   250	  // Auth
   251	  user: null,
   252	  stage: getAccessToken() ? "shift-open" : "login",
   253	  loading: false,
   254	  error: null,
   255	  clearError: () => set({ error: null }),
   256	
   257	  // Mode
   258	  mode: "sale",
   259	  setMode: (m) => set({ mode: m }),
   260	
   261	  // Data
   262	  products: [],
   263	  productsLoading: false,
   264	
   265	  // Customer
   266	  selectedCustomer: null,
   267	  customerSearchResults: [],
   268	  customerSearching: false,
   269	
   270	  // Cart
   271	  cart: [],
   272	
   273	  // Wastage
   274	  wastage: [],
   275	  wastageDraft: [],
   276	
   277	  // Held Orders
   278	  heldOrders: [],
   279	
   280	
   281	  // Transaction
   282	  lastTransaction: null,
   283	  scanFlash: 0,
   284	
   285	  // Shift
   286	  shift: null,
   287	  shiftSummary: null,
   288	
   289	  // Return / Refund
   290	  lookedUpTx: null,
   291	  returnLoading: false,
   292	  returnError: null,
   293	  lastRefund: null,
   294	
   295	  // ── Auth Actions ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   296	
   297	  login: async (employeeId, pin) => {
   298	    set({ loading: true, error: null });
   299	    try {
   300	      const res = await pos.posLogin({ employee_id: employeeId, pin });
   301	      // SDK's posLogin automatically stores tokens via setAuthTokens
   302	      set({
   303	        user: { employeeId, name: res.employee_name },
   304	        stage: "shift-open",
   305	        loading: false,
   306	      });
   307	      return true;
   308	    } catch (err: any) {
   309	      const message =
   310	        err?.response?.data?.error || err?.message || "Login failed";
   311	      set({ error: message, loading: false });
   312	      return false;
   313	    }
   314	  },
   315	
   316	  logout: () => {
   317	    clearAuthTokens();
   318	    set({
   319	      user: null,
   320	      stage: "login",
   321	      cart: [],
   322	      selectedCustomer: null,
   323	      customerSearchResults: [],
   324	      lastTransaction: null,
   325	      wastageDraft: [],
   326	      mode: "sale",
   327	      shift: null,
   328	      shiftSummary: null,
   329	      products: [],
   330	      error: null,
   331	    });
   332	  },
   333	
   334	  // ── Shift Actions ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   335	
   336	  openShift: async (openingCash) => {
   337	    const { user } = get();
   338	    if (!user) return;
   339	
   340	    set({ loading: true, error: null });
   341	    try {
   342	      const res = await pos.openShift({
   343	        employee_id: user.employeeId,
   344	        opening_cash: openingCash,
   345	      });
   346	
   347	      set({
   348	        stage: "pos",
   349	        shift: {
   350	          id: res.shift_id,
   351	          startedAt: Date.now(),
   352	          openingCash,
   353	          cashSales: 0,
   354	          totalSales: 0,
   355	          txnCount: 0,
   356	          refundTotal: 0,
   357	        },
   358	        loading: false,
   359	      });
   360	
   361	      // Auto-fetch products after opening shift
   362	      get().fetchProducts();
   363	    } catch (err: any) {
   364	      const message =
   365	        err?.response?.data?.error || err?.message || "Failed to open shift";
   366	      set({ error: message, loading: false });
   367	    }
   368	  },
   369	
   370	  closeShift: () => set({ stage: "shift-close" }),
   371	
   372	  submitCloseShift: async (closingCash, notes) => {
   373	    set({ loading: true, error: null });
   374	    try {
   375	      const summary = await pos.closeShift({
   376	        closing_cash: closingCash,
   377	        notes,
   378	      });
   379	
   380	      set({ shiftSummary: summary, loading: false });
   381	    } catch (err: any) {
   382	      const message =
   383	        err?.response?.data?.error || err?.message || "Failed to close shift";
   384	      set({ error: message, loading: false });
   385	    }
   386	  },
   387	
   388	  finishCloseShift: () => {
   389	    clearAuthTokens();
   390	    set({
   391	      shift: null,
   392	      shiftSummary: null,
   393	      user: null,
   394	      stage: "login",
   395	      cart: [],
   396	      wastageDraft: [],
   397	      selectedCustomer: null,
   398	      customerSearchResults: [],
   399	      mode: "sale",
   400	      products: [],
   401	      error: null,
   402	    });
   403	  },
   404	
   405	  // ── Product Catalog ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   406	
   407	  fetchProducts: async (params) => {
   408	    set({ productsLoading: true });
   409	    try {
   410	      const products = await pos.getProducts(params);
   411	      set({ products, productsLoading: false });
   412	    } catch (err: any) {
   413	      console.error("[POS] Failed to fetch products:", err);
   414	      set({ productsLoading: false });
   415	    }
   416	  },
   417	
   418	  // ── Customer Actions ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   419	
   420	  searchCustomer: async (phone) => {
   421	    if (phone.length < 3) {
   422	      set({ customerSearchResults: [] });
   423	      return;
   424	    }
   425	
   426	    set({ customerSearching: true });
   427	    try {
   428	      const customer = await pos.lookupCustomer(phone);
   429	      set({
   430	        customerSearchResults: customer ? [customer] : [],
   431	        customerSearching: false,
   432	      });
   433	    } catch {
   434	      set({ customerSearchResults: [], customerSearching: false });
   435	    }
   436	  },
   437	
   438	  selectCustomer: (c) => set({ selectedCustomer: c, customerSearchResults: [] }),
   439	
   440	  addCustomer: async (data) => {
   441	    set({ loading: true, error: null });
   442	    try {
   443	      const customer = await pos.addCustomer(data);
   444	      set({
   445	        selectedCustomer: customer,
   446	        customerSearchResults: [],
   447	        loading: false,
   448	      });
   449	      return customer;
   450	    } catch (err: any) {
   451	      const message =
   452	        err?.response?.data?.error || err?.message || "Failed to add customer";
   453	      set({ error: message, loading: false });
   454	      return null;
   455	    }
   456	  },
   457	
   458	  clearCustomerSearch: () => set({ customerSearchResults: [] }),
   459	
   460	  // ── Cart Actions ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   461	
   462	  scan: (pid, weight) => {
   463	    const p = get().products.find((x) => x.pid === pid);
   464	    if (!p) return false;
   465	    const qty = p.weighed ? weight ?? 1 : 1;
   466	    if (get().mode === "wastage") get().addWastageDraft(p, qty);
   467	    else get().addProduct(p, qty);
   468	    set({ scanFlash: Date.now() });
   469	    return true;
   470	  },
   471	
   472	  addProduct: (p, qty = 1) => {
   473	    set((s) => {
   474	      const existing = s.cart.find((i) => i.pid === p.pid);
   475	      if (existing) {
   476	        return {
   477	          cart: s.cart.map((i) =>
   478	            i.pid === p.pid
   479	              ? { ...i, quantity: +(i.quantity + qty).toFixed(3) }
   480	              : i
   481	          ),
   482	        };
   483	      }
   484	      return {
   485	        cart: [
   486	          ...s.cart,
   487	          {
   488	            pid: p.pid,
   489	            name: p.name,
   490	            unitPrice: p.price,
   491	            weighed: p.weighed,
   492	            quantity: qty,
   493	            memberEligible: p.member_eligible,
   494	          },
   495	        ],
   496	      };
   497	    });
   498	  },
   499	
   500	  setQty: (pid, qty) =>
   501	    set((s) => ({
   502	      cart: s.cart.map((i) =>
   503	        i.pid === pid ? { ...i, quantity: Math.max(0.01, qty) } : i
   504	      ),
   505	    })),
   506	
   507	  removeItem: (pid) =>
   508	    set((s) => ({ cart: s.cart.filter((i) => i.pid !== pid) })),
   509	
   510	  clearCart: () => set({ cart: [] }),
   511	
   512	  // ── Wastage Actions ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   513	
   514	  addWastageDraft: (p, qty = 1) => {
   515	    set((s) => {
   516	      const existing = s.wastageDraft.find((i) => i.pid === p.pid);
   517	      if (existing) {
   518	        return {
   519	          wastageDraft: s.wastageDraft.map((i) =>
   520	            i.pid === p.pid
   521	              ? { ...i, quantity: +(i.quantity + qty).toFixed(3) }
   522	              : i
   523	          ),
   524	        };
   525	      }
   526	      return {
   527	        wastageDraft: [
   528	          ...s.wastageDraft,
   529	          {
   530	            pid: p.pid,
   531	            name: p.name,
   532	            quantity: qty,
   533	            weighed: p.weighed,
   534	            unitPrice: p.price,
   535	          },
   536	        ],
   537	      };
   538	    });
   539	  },
   540	
   541	  setWastageQty: (pid, qty) =>
   542	    set((s) => ({
   543	      wastageDraft: s.wastageDraft.map((i) =>
   544	        i.pid === pid ? { ...i, quantity: Math.max(0.01, qty) } : i
   545	      ),
   546	    })),
   547	
   548	  removeWastageDraft: (pid) =>
   549	    set((s) => ({
   550	      wastageDraft: s.wastageDraft.filter((i) => i.pid !== pid),
   551	    })),
   552	
   553	  clearWastageDraft: () => set({ wastageDraft: [] }),
   554	
   555	  submitWastage: async (reason) => {
   556	    const draft = get().wastageDraft;
   557	    if (draft.length === 0) return;
   558	
   559	    set({ loading: true, error: null });
   560	
   561	    try {
   562	      // Submit each wastage entry to backend
   563	      for (const d of draft) {
   564	        await pos.logWastage({
   565	          pid: d.pid,
   566	          name: d.name,
   567	          quantity: d.quantity,
   568	          weighed: d.weighed,
   569	          unit_price: d.unitPrice,
   570	          reason,
   571	        });
   572	      }
   573	
   574	      const ts = Date.now();
   575	      const entries: WastageEntry[] = draft.map((d) => ({
   576	        ...d,
   577	        reason,
   578	        timestamp: ts,
   579	      }));
   580	
   581	      set((s) => ({
   582	        wastage: [...entries, ...s.wastage],
   583	        products: s.products.map((p) => {
   584	          const e = entries.find((x) => x.pid === p.pid);
   585	          return e
   586	            ? { ...p, stock: Math.max(0, +(p.stock - e.quantity).toFixed(3)) }
   587	            : p;
   588	        }),
   589	        wastageDraft: [],
   590	        mode: "sale" as const,
   591	        loading: false,
   592	      }));
   593	    } catch (err: any) {
   594	      const message =
   595	        err?.response?.data?.error || err?.message || "Failed to log wastage";
   596	      set({ error: message, loading: false });
   597	    }
   598	  },
   599	
   600	  // ── Stage & Payment ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   601	
   602	  setStage: (s) => set({ stage: s }),
   603	
   604	  pay: async (tenders, bharatpeTxnId) => {
   605	    const { cart, selectedCustomer, shift } = get();
   606	    if (!selectedCustomer || cart.length === 0 || tenders.length === 0)
   607	      return null;
   608	
   609	    const pride = !!selectedCustomer.pride;
   610	    const subtotal = +subtotalOf(cart, pride).toFixed(2);
   611	    const gross = +grossSubtotalOf(cart).toFixed(2);
   612	    const memberDiscount = +(gross - subtotal).toFixed(2);
   613	
   614	    const sodexoTender = tenders.find((t) => t.method === "Sodexo");
   615	    const surchargeSimple = sodexoTender
   616	      ? +(sodexoTender.amount * 0.05).toFixed(2)
   617	      : 0;
   618	    const total = +(subtotal + surchargeSimple).toFixed(2);
   619	    const cashAmt = tenders
   620	      .filter((t) => t.method === "Cash")
   621	      .reduce((s, t) => s + t.amount, 0);
   622	    const isSplit = tenders.length > 1;
   623	    const method = isSplit ? ("Split" as const) : tenders[0].method;
   624	
   625	    set({ loading: true, error: null });
   626	
   627	    try {
   628	      // Map cart items to SDK format (snake_case)
   629	      const sdkItems = cart.map((i) => ({
   630	        pid: i.pid,
   631	        name: i.name,
   632	        unit_price: memberPriceOf(i, pride),
   633	        weighed: i.weighed,
   634	        quantity: i.quantity,
   635	        member_eligible: i.memberEligible,
   636	      }));
   637	
   638	      const sdkTenders = tenders.map((t) => ({
   639	        method: t.method,
   640	        amount: t.amount,
   641	      }));
   642	
   643	      // Submit to backend
   644	      const backendTx = await pos.createOrder({
   645	        customer_id: String(selectedCustomer.id),
   646	        items: sdkItems,
   647	        tenders: sdkTenders,
   648	        subtotal,
   649	        member_discount: memberDiscount,
   650	        surcharge: surchargeSimple,
   651	        total,
   652	      });
   653	
   654	      // Build local transaction from backend response
   655	      const tx: Transaction = {
   656	        id: backendTx.id,
   657	        customerId: String(selectedCustomer.id),
   658	        items: cart,
   659	        tenders,
   660	        method,
   661	        subtotal,
   662	        memberDiscount,
   663	        surcharge: surchargeSimple,
   664	        total,
   665	        timestamp: backendTx.timestamp || Date.now(),
   666	        receiptDelivery: "Print",
   667	        bharatpeTxnId,
   668	      };
   669	
   670	      set((s) => ({
   671	        lastTransaction: tx,
   672	        stage: "receipt" as const,
   673	        loading: false,
   674	        shift: s.shift
   675	          ? {
   676	              ...s.shift,
   677	              cashSales: +(s.shift.cashSales + cashAmt).toFixed(2),
   678	              totalSales: +(s.shift.totalSales + total).toFixed(2),
   679	              txnCount: s.shift.txnCount + 1,
   680	            }
   681	          : s.shift,
   682	        products: s.products.map((p) => {
   683	          const ci = cart.find((c) => c.pid === p.pid);
   684	          return ci
   685	            ? { ...p, stock: Math.max(0, +(p.stock - ci.quantity).toFixed(3)) }
   686	            : p;
   687	        }),
   688	      }));
   689	
   690	      return tx;
   691	    } catch (err: any) {
   692	      const message =
   693	        err?.response?.data?.error || err?.message || "Order submission failed";
   694	      set({ error: message, loading: false });
   695	      return null;
   696	    }
   697	  },
   698	  setReceiptDelivery: (d) =>
   699	    set((s) => ({
   700	      lastTransaction: s.lastTransaction
   701	        ? { ...s.lastTransaction, receiptDelivery: d }
   702	        : null,
   703	    })),
   704	
   705	  // ── Held Orders Actions ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   706	
   707	  holdCart: () => {
   708	    const { cart, selectedCustomer, heldOrders } = get();
   709	    if (cart.length === 0) return;
   710	
   711	    const newHeldOrder: HeldOrder = {
   712	      id: Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 9).toUpperCase(),
   713	      cart: [...cart],
   714	      customer: selectedCustomer,
   715	      timestamp: Date.now(),
   716	    };
   717	
   718	    set({
   719	      heldOrders: [newHeldOrder, ...heldOrders],
   720	      cart: [],
   721	      selectedCustomer: null,
   722	    });
   723	  },
   724	
   725	  resumeHeldOrder: (id) => {
   726	    const { heldOrders, cart } = get();
   727	    const order = heldOrders.find((o) => o.id === id);
   728	    if (!order) return;
   729	
   730	    // If current cart is not empty, we might want to hold it first? 
   731	    // For now, we just swap.
   732	    set({
   733	      cart: order.cart,
   734	      selectedCustomer: order.customer,
   735	      heldOrders: heldOrders.filter((o) => o.id !== id),
   736	    });
   737	  },
   738	
   739	  deleteHeldOrder: (id) => {
   740	    set((s) => ({
   741	      heldOrders: s.heldOrders.filter((o) => o.id !== id),
   742	    }));
   743	  },
   744	
   745	  // ── Return / Refund Actions ──────────────────────────────────────────
   746	
   747	  lookupTransaction: async (receiptId) => {
   748	    set({ returnLoading: true, returnError: null, lookedUpTx: null });
   749	    try {
   750	      const tx = await pos.lookupTransaction(receiptId);
   751	
   752	      const items: ReturnItem[] = (tx.items || []).map((i: any) => ({
   753	        pid: i.pid,
   754	        name: i.name,
   755	        unitPrice: Number(i.unit_price),
   756	        weighed: i.weighed,
   757	        originalQty: Number(i.quantity),
   758	        returnQty: Number(i.quantity),
   759	        selected: true,
   760	      }));
   761	
   762	      set({
   763	        lookedUpTx: {
   764	          id: tx.id,
   765	          items,
   766	          method: tx.method,
   767	          subtotal: Number(tx.subtotal),
   768	          total: Number(tx.total),
   769	          timestamp: tx.timestamp || Date.now(),
   770	          customerName: tx.customer_name,
   771	        },
   772	        returnLoading: false,
   773	        stage: "return",
   774	      });
   775	      return true;
   776	    } catch (err: any) {
   777	      const message =
   778	        err?.response?.data?.error || err?.message || "Transaction not found";
   779	      set({ returnError: message, returnLoading: false });
   780	      return false;
   781	    }
   782	  },
   783	
   784	  toggleReturnItem: (pid) => {
   785	    set((s) => ({
   786	      lookedUpTx: s.lookedUpTx
   787	        ? {
   788	            ...s.lookedUpTx,
   789	            items: s.lookedUpTx.items.map((i) =>
   790	              i.pid === pid ? { ...i, selected: !i.selected } : i
   791	            ),
   792	          }
   793	        : null,
   794	    }));
   795	  },
   796	
   797	  setReturnQty: (pid, qty) => {
   798	    set((s) => ({
   799	      lookedUpTx: s.lookedUpTx
   800	        ? {
   801	            ...s.lookedUpTx,
   802	            items: s.lookedUpTx.items.map((i) =>
   803	              i.pid === pid
   804	                ? { ...i, returnQty: Math.min(Math.max(0.01, qty), i.originalQty) }
   805	                : i
   806	            ),
   807	          }
   808	        : null,
   809	    }));
   810	  },
   811	
   812	  processRefund: async (managerPin, refundMethod) => {
   813	    const { lookedUpTx, shift } = get();
   814	    if (!lookedUpTx) return false;
   815	
   816	    const selectedItems = lookedUpTx.items.filter((i) => i.selected);
   817	    if (selectedItems.length === 0) return false;
   818	
   819	    set({ returnLoading: true, returnError: null });
   820	
   821	    try {
   822	      const result = await pos.processRefund({
   823	        original_transaction_id: lookedUpTx.id,
   824	        manager_pin: managerPin,
   825	        items: selectedItems.map((i) => ({
   826	          pid: i.pid,
   827	          quantity: i.returnQty,
   828	        })),
   829	        refund_method: refundMethod,
   830	      });
   831	
   832	      const refundTotal = Math.abs(Number(result.total));
   833	
   834	      const refundTx: Transaction = {
   835	        id: result.id,
   836	        customerId: "",
   837	        items: selectedItems.map((i) => ({
   838	          pid: i.pid,
   839	          name: i.name,
   840	          unitPrice: i.unitPrice,
   841	          weighed: i.weighed,
   842	          quantity: i.returnQty,
   843	        })),
   844	        tenders: [{ method: refundMethod, amount: refundTotal }],
   845	        method: refundMethod,
   846	        subtotal: -refundTotal,
   847	        memberDiscount: 0,
   848	        surcharge: 0,
   849	        total: -refundTotal,
   850	        timestamp: Date.now(),
   851	        transactionType: "RETURN",
   852	        relatedTransactionId: lookedUpTx.id,
   853	      };
   854	
   855	      set((s) => ({
   856	        lastRefund: refundTx,
   857	        lastTransaction: refundTx,
   858	        stage: "receipt" as const,
   859	        returnLoading: false,
   860	        lookedUpTx: null,
   861	        shift: s.shift
   862	          ? {
   863	              ...s.shift,
   864	              refundTotal: +(s.shift.refundTotal + refundTotal).toFixed(2),
   865	              totalSales: +(s.shift.totalSales - refundTotal).toFixed(2),
   866	              cashSales:
   867	                refundMethod === "Cash"
   868	                  ? +(s.shift.cashSales - refundTotal).toFixed(2)
   869	                  : s.shift.cashSales,
   870	              txnCount: s.shift.txnCount + 1,
   871	            }
   872	          : s.shift,
   873	        // Restock products locally
   874	        products: s.products.map((p) => {
   875	          const ri = selectedItems.find((x) => x.pid === p.pid);
   876	          return ri
   877	            ? { ...p, stock: +(p.stock + ri.returnQty).toFixed(3) }
   878	            : p;
   879	        }),
   880	      }));
   881	
   882	      return true;
   883	    } catch (err: any) {
   884	      const message =
   885	        err?.response?.data?.error || err?.message || "Refund failed";
   886	      set({ returnError: message, returnLoading: false });
   887	      return false;
   888	    }
   889	  },
   890	
   891	  clearReturn: () => set({
   892	    lookedUpTx: null,
   893	    returnError: null,
   894	    returnLoading: false,
   895	    lastRefund: null,
   896	    stage: "pos" as const,
   897	  }),
   898	}));

     1	import { useCallback, useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from "react";
     2	import { usePos, subtotalOf, formatINR } from "../store";
     3	import type { PaymentMethod, Tender } from "../store";
     4	import { invoke } from "@tauri-apps/api/core";
     5	import {
     6	  generateUPIQR, pushToCardMachine, pollUntilResolved,
     7	  type BharatPePaymentStatus,
     8	} from "../bharatpe";
     9	import {
    10	  Banknote, Smartphone, CreditCard, Sparkles, X, AlertTriangle,
    11	  SplitSquareHorizontal, Plus, Trash2, Loader2, CheckCircle2, QrCode,
    12	  WifiOff, XCircle, ShieldCheck,
    13	} from "lucide-react";
    14	import { QRCodeSVG } from "qrcode.react";
    15	
    16	const ICON: Record<PaymentMethod, any> = {
    17	  Cash: Banknote, UPI: Smartphone, Card: CreditCard, Sodexo: Sparkles,
    18	};
    19	
    20	type BPStep = "idle" | "generating" | "qr-shown" | "polling" | "card-pushed" | "success" | "failed";
    21	
    22	/** Extended tender with per-item BharatPe verification status */
    23	interface SplitTender extends Tender {
    24	  bpStep: BPStep;
    25	  bpTxnId: string;
    26	  bpQR: string;
    27	}
    28	
    29	const isDigital = (m: PaymentMethod) => m === "UPI" || m === "Card";
    30	
    31	export default function PaymentDrawer() {
    32	  const cart = usePos((s) => s.cart);
    33	  const customer = usePos((s) => s.selectedCustomer);
    34	  const setStage = usePos((s) => s.setStage);
    35	  const pay = usePos((s) => s.pay);
    36	  const loading = usePos((s) => s.loading);
    37	  const error = usePos((s) => s.error);
    38	
    39	  const [split, setSplit] = useState(false);
    40	  const [method, setMethod] = useState<PaymentMethod>("Cash");
    41	  const [draftMethod, setDraftMethod] = useState<PaymentMethod>("Cash");
    42	  const [draftAmt, setDraftAmt] = useState("");
    43	
    44	  // ── Single-mode BharatPe state ──
    45	  const [bpStep, setBpStep] = useState<BPStep>("idle");
    46	  const [bpQR, setBpQR] = useState("");
    47	  const [bpTxnId, setBpTxnId] = useState("");
    48	  const [bpStatus, setBpStatus] = useState<BharatPePaymentStatus>("CREATED");
    49	  const [bpError, setBpError] = useState("");
    50	  const pollCancelRef = useRef(false);
    51	
    52	  // ── Split-mode state with per-tender verification ──
    53	  const [splitTenders, setSplitTenders] = useState<SplitTender[]>([]);
    54	  const [activeSplitIdx, setActiveSplitIdx] = useState<number | null>(null);
    55	  const splitPollCancelRef = useRef(false);
    56	
    57	  const pride = !!customer?.pride;
    58	  const subtotal = subtotalOf(cart, pride);
    59	  const singleSurcharge = method === "Sodexo" ? +(subtotal * 0.05).toFixed(2) : 0;
    60	  const singleTotal = +(subtotal + singleSurcharge).toFixed(2);
    61	
    62	  const splitSodexo = splitTenders.filter((t) => t.method === "Sodexo").reduce((s, t) => s + t.amount, 0);
    63	  const splitSurcharge = +(splitSodexo * 0.05).toFixed(2);
    64	  const splitTotalDue = +(subtotal + splitSurcharge).toFixed(2);
    65	  const splitPaid = splitTenders.reduce((s, t) => s + t.amount, 0);
    66	  const splitRemaining = +(splitTotalDue - splitPaid).toFixed(2);
    67	
    68	  // Is any split tender currently being verified?
    69	  const splitVerifying = activeSplitIdx !== null;
    70	  const hasUnverifiedDigital = splitTenders.some((t) => isDigital(t.method) && t.bpStep !== "success");
    71	
    72	  // Cleanup on unmount
    73	  useEffect(() => {
    74	    return () => { pollCancelRef.current = true; splitPollCancelRef.current = true; };
    75	  }, []);
    76	
    77	  // ── Single-mode BharatPe flows ──
    78	  const startUPIFlow = useCallback(async (amount: number) => {
    79	    setBpStep("generating"); setBpError("");
    80	    try {
    81	      const qr = await generateUPIQR(amount);
    82	      setBpQR(qr.qr_string); setBpTxnId(qr.transaction_id);
    83	      setBpStep("polling"); pollCancelRef.current = false;
    84	      const result = await pollUntilResolved(qr.transaction_id, (s) => {
    85	        if (!pollCancelRef.current) setBpStatus(s.status);
    86	      }, 60, 3000);
    87	      if (pollCancelRef.current) return;
    88	      setBpStep(result.status === "SUCCESS" ? "success" : "failed");
    89	      if (result.status !== "SUCCESS") setBpError(`Payment ${result.status.toLowerCase()}`);
    90	    } catch (err: any) { setBpStep("failed"); setBpError(err?.message || "UPI failed"); }
    91	  }, []);
    92	
    93	  const startCardFlow = useCallback(async (amount: number) => {
    94	    setBpStep("generating"); setBpError("");
    95	    try {
    96	      const res = await pushToCardMachine(amount);
    97	      setBpTxnId(res.transaction_id); setBpStep("card-pushed");
    98	      pollCancelRef.current = false;
    99	      const result = await pollUntilResolved(res.transaction_id, (s) => {
   100	        if (!pollCancelRef.current) setBpStatus(s.status);
   101	      }, 60, 3000);
   102	      if (pollCancelRef.current) return;
   103	      setBpStep(result.status === "SUCCESS" ? "success" : "failed");
   104	      if (result.status !== "SUCCESS") setBpError(`Card ${result.status.toLowerCase()}`);
   105	    } catch (err: any) { setBpStep("failed"); setBpError(err?.message || "Card failed"); }
   106	  }, []);
   107	
   108	  // Auto-trigger for single mode
   109	  useEffect(() => {
   110	    if (split || bpStep !== "idle") return;
   111	    if (method === "UPI") startUPIFlow(singleTotal);
   112	    else if (method === "Card") startCardFlow(singleTotal);
   113	  }, [method, split, singleTotal, bpStep, startUPIFlow, startCardFlow]);
   114	
   115	  const resetBP = () => {
   116	    pollCancelRef.current = true;
   117	    setBpStep("idle"); setBpQR(""); setBpTxnId(""); setBpStatus("CREATED"); setBpError("");
   118	  };
   119	
   120	  const handleMethodChange = (m: PaymentMethod) => { resetBP(); setMethod(m); };
   121	
   122	  // ── Split-mode: verify a specific digital tender ──
   123	  const verifySplitTender = useCallback(async (idx: number) => {
   124	    const t = splitTenders[idx];
   125	    if (!t || !isDigital(t.method)) return;
   126	
   127	    setActiveSplitIdx(idx);
   128	    splitPollCancelRef.current = false;
   129	
   130	    // Update tender step
   131	    const update = (patch: Partial<SplitTender>) =>
   132	      setSplitTenders((prev) => prev.map((x, i) => i === idx ? { ...x, ...patch } : x));
   133	
   134	    update({ bpStep: "generating" });
   135	
   136	    try {
   137	      if (t.method === "UPI") {
   138	        const qr = await generateUPIQR(t.amount);
   139	        update({ bpQR: qr.qr_string, bpTxnId: qr.transaction_id, bpStep: "polling" });
   140	        const result = await pollUntilResolved(qr.transaction_id, () => {}, 60, 3000);
   141	        if (splitPollCancelRef.current) return;
   142	        update({ bpStep: result.status === "SUCCESS" ? "success" : "failed" });
   143	      } else {
   144	        const res = await pushToCardMachine(t.amount);
   145	        update({ bpTxnId: res.transaction_id, bpStep: "card-pushed" });
   146	        const result = await pollUntilResolved(res.transaction_id, () => {}, 60, 3000);
   147	        if (splitPollCancelRef.current) return;
   148	        update({ bpStep: result.status === "SUCCESS" ? "success" : "failed" });
   149	      }
   150	    } catch {
   151	      update({ bpStep: "failed" });
   152	    }
   153	    setActiveSplitIdx(null);
   154	  }, [splitTenders]);
   155	
   156	  // Auto-verify next unverified digital tender sequentially
   157	  useEffect(() => {
   158	    if (!split || splitVerifying) return;
   159	    const nextIdx = splitTenders.findIndex((t) => isDigital(t.method) && t.bpStep === "idle");
   160	    if (nextIdx !== -1) verifySplitTender(nextIdx);
   161	  }, [split, splitTenders, splitVerifying, verifySplitTender]);
   162	
   163	  const addTender = () => {
   164	    const amt = parseFloat(draftAmt);
   165	    if (!amt || amt <= 0 || splitVerifying) return;
   166	    setSplitTenders([...splitTenders, {
   167	      method: draftMethod, amount: +amt.toFixed(2),
   168	      bpStep: isDigital(draftMethod) ? "idle" : "success", // non-digital auto-verified
   169	      bpTxnId: "", bpQR: "",
   170	    }]);
   171	    setDraftAmt("");
   172	  };
   173	
   174	  const removeSplitTender = (idx: number) => {
   175	    const t = splitTenders[idx];
   176	    if (activeSplitIdx === idx) { splitPollCancelRef.current = true; setActiveSplitIdx(null); }
   177	    setSplitTenders(splitTenders.filter((_, i) => i !== idx));
   178	  };
   179	
   180	  // Collect all BharatPe txn IDs for the order
   181	  const allBpTxnIds = useMemo(() => {
   182	    if (!split) return bpTxnId || undefined;
   183	    const ids = splitTenders.filter((t) => t.bpTxnId).map((t) => t.bpTxnId);
   184	    return ids.length ? ids.join(",") : undefined;
   185	  }, [split, bpTxnId, splitTenders]);
   186	
   187	  const confirm = async () => {
   188	    // Check if any tender is Cash
   189	    const hasCash = split
   190	      ? splitTenders.some((t) => t.method === "Cash")
   191	      : method === "Cash";
   192	    if (hasCash) {
   193	      await invoke("open_cash_drawer").catch(console.error);
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    if (split) {
   197	      if (Math.abs(splitRemaining) > 0.01 || hasUnverifiedDigital) return;
   198	      const tenders: Tender[] = splitTenders.map((t) => ({ method: t.method, amount: t.amount }));
   199	      await pay(tenders, allBpTxnIds);
   200	    } else {
   201	      if (isDigital(method) && bpStep !== "success") return;
   202	      await pay([{ method, amount: singleTotal }], allBpTxnIds);
   203	    }
   204	  };
   205	
   206	  const canConfirm = useMemo(() => {
   207	    if (loading) return false;
   208	    if (split) return Math.abs(splitRemaining) <= 0.01 && !hasUnverifiedDigital;
   209	    if (isDigital(method)) return bpStep === "success";
   210	    return true;
   211	  }, [loading, split, splitRemaining, hasUnverifiedDigital, method, bpStep]);
   212	
   213	  // ── Shared UI helpers ──
   214	  const Btn = ({ m, label, special, active, onClick, disabled }: {
   215	    m: PaymentMethod; label: string; special?: boolean; active: boolean; onClick: () => void; disabled?: boolean;
   216	  }) => {
   217	    const I = ICON[m];
   218	    return (
   219	      <button onClick={onClick} disabled={disabled}
   220	        className={`pressable border-2 border-foreground p-3 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1 h-24 font-extrabold
   221	          ${active ? (special ? "bg-sodexo text-sodexo-foreground" : "bg-primary text-primary-foreground")
   222	                   : (special ? "bg-card text-sodexo border-sodexo" : "bg-card hover:bg-secondary")}
   223	          ${disabled ? "opacity-40 cursor-not-allowed" : ""}`}>
   224	        <I size={26}/>
   225	        <span className="tracking-widest text-xs">{label}</span>
   226	      </button>
   227	    );
   228	  };
   229	
   230	  /** Render BharatPe status for a specific amount/step/qr/txnId/method */
   231	  const renderBPPanel = (pMethod: PaymentMethod, step: BPStep, qr: string, txnId: string, amount: number, onRetry?: () => void) => {
   232	    if (!isDigital(pMethod)) return null;
   233	    return (
   234	      <div className="border-2 border-foreground mb-3 bg-background">
   235	        {pMethod === "UPI" && (step === "qr-shown" || step === "polling") && qr && (
   236	          <div className="flex flex-col items-center p-4 gap-2">
   237	            <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest flex items-center gap-2">
   238	              <QrCode size={14}/> SCAN TO PAY · BHARATPE
   239	            </div>
   240	            <div className="bg-white p-3 border-2 border-foreground">
   241	              <QRCodeSVG value={qr} size={180} level="H" />
   242	            </div>
   243	            <div className="font-mono font-extrabold text-xl tabular-nums">{formatINR(amount)}</div>
   244	            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-accent">
   245	              <Loader2 size={14} className="animate-spin"/>
   246	              <span className="font-extrabold text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest">Waiting for payment...</span>
   247	            </div>
   248	            <div className="font-mono text-[9px] text-muted-foreground">TXN: {txnId}</div>
   249	          </div>
   250	        )}
   251	        {pMethod === "Card" && step === "card-pushed" && (
   252	          <div className="flex flex-col items-center p-4 gap-2">
   253	            <CreditCard size={32} className="text-primary"/>
   254	            <div className="font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-xs">Pushed to Card Machine</div>
   255	            <div className="font-mono font-extrabold text-2xl tabular-nums">{formatINR(amount)}</div>
   256	            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-accent">
   257	              <Loader2 size={14} className="animate-spin"/>
   258	              <span className="font-extrabold text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest">Waiting for tap/insert...</span>
   259	            </div>
   260	          </div>
   261	        )}
   262	        {step === "generating" && (
   263	          <div className="flex flex-col items-center p-4 gap-2">
   264	            <Loader2 size={28} className="animate-spin text-primary"/>
   265	            <span className="font-extrabold text-xs uppercase tracking-widest">
   266	              {pMethod === "UPI" ? "Generating QR..." : "Connecting..."}
   267	            </span>
   268	          </div>
   269	        )}
   270	        {step === "success" && (
   271	          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-primary text-primary-foreground">
   272	            <CheckCircle2 size={22}/> <span className="font-extrabold text-xs uppercase tracking-widest">Verified</span>
   273	            <span className="font-mono text-[10px] ml-auto">TXN: {txnId}</span>
   274	          </div>
   275	        )}
   276	        {step === "failed" && (
   277	          <div className="flex flex-col items-center p-3 gap-2 bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground">
   278	            <XCircle size={24}/>
   279	            <span className="font-extrabold text-xs uppercase tracking-widest">Payment Failed</span>
   280	            {onRetry && (
   281	              <button onClick={onRetry} className="pressable border-2 border-destructive-foreground px-3 py-1 font-extrabold text-[10px] tracking-widest">RETRY</button>
   282	            )}
   283	          </div>
   284	        )}
   285	      </div>
   286	    );
   287	  };
   288	
   289	  // ── Split tender status badge ──
   290	  const tenderBadge = (t: SplitTender) => {
   291	    if (!isDigital(t.method)) return <ShieldCheck size={14} className="text-primary"/>;
   292	    if (t.bpStep === "success") return <CheckCircle2 size={14} className="text-primary"/>;
   293	    if (t.bpStep === "failed") return <XCircle size={14} className="text-destructive"/>;
   294	    if (t.bpStep === "idle") return <span className="w-3 h-3 border-2 border-foreground bg-muted"/>;
   295	    return <Loader2 size={14} className="animate-spin text-accent"/>;
   296	  };
   297	
   298	  return (
   299	    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-foreground/80 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
   300	      <div className="border-sharp-3 bg-card w-[720px] max-h-[720px] overflow-y-auto scrollbar-sharp" style={{ boxShadow: "10px 10px 0 0 hsl(var(--foreground))" }}>
   301	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between bg-foreground text-background px-5 py-3 border-b-2 border-foreground">
   302	          <h2 className="text-2xl font-extrabold uppercase tracking-tight">Payment</h2>
   303	          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
   304	            <button onClick={() => { setSplit(!split); setSplitTenders([]); resetBP(); setActiveSplitIdx(null); splitPollCancelRef.current = true; }}
   305	              className={`pressable border-2 border-background px-3 py-1.5 font-extrabold text-xs tracking-widest flex items-center gap-2
   306	                ${split ? "bg-accent text-accent-foreground" : "bg-foreground text-background"}`}>
   307	              <SplitSquareHorizontal size={16}/> SPLIT {split ? "ON" : "OFF"}
   308	            </button>
   309	            <button onClick={() => { resetBP(); splitPollCancelRef.current = true; setStage("pos"); }} className="border-2 border-background p-1 hover:bg-destructive">
   310	              <X size={20}/>
   311	            </button>
   312	          </div>
   313	        </div>
   314	
   315	        <div className="p-5">
   316	          {!split ? (
   317	            <>
   318	              <div className="text-[11px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">Select Method</div>
   319	              <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-3 mb-5">
   320	                <Btn m="Cash" label="CASH" active={method==="Cash"} onClick={() => handleMethodChange("Cash")}/>
   321	                <Btn m="UPI" label="UPI" active={method==="UPI"} onClick={() => handleMethodChange("UPI")}/>
   322	                <Btn m="Card" label="CARD" active={method==="Card"} onClick={() => handleMethodChange("Card")}/>
   323	                <Btn m="Sodexo" label="SODEXO" special active={method==="Sodexo"} onClick={() => handleMethodChange("Sodexo")}/>
   324	              </div>
   325	              {isDigital(method) && renderBPPanel(method, bpStep, bpQR, bpTxnId, singleTotal, resetBP)}
   326	            </>
   327	          ) : (
   328	            <>
   329	              <div className="text-[11px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">Split Tenders</div>
   330	              <div className="border-2 border-foreground bg-background p-3 mb-3">
   331	                <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mb-3">
   332	                  {(["Cash","UPI","Card","Sodexo"] as PaymentMethod[]).map((m) => (
   333	                    <Btn key={m} m={m} label={m.toUpperCase()} special={m==="Sodexo"} active={draftMethod===m}
   334	                      disabled={splitVerifying} onClick={() => setDraftMethod(m)}/>
   335	                  ))}
   336	                </div>
   337	                <div className="flex gap-2">
   338	                  <input type="number" inputMode="decimal" value={draftAmt}
   339	                    onChange={(e) => setDraftAmt(e.target.value)} disabled={splitVerifying}
   340	                    placeholder={`AMOUNT (REMAINING ${formatINR(Math.max(0, splitRemaining))})`}
   341	                    className="flex-1 border-2 border-foreground bg-background px-3 py-2 font-mono font-bold text-base outline-none focus:border-primary disabled:opacity-50"/>
   342	                  <button onClick={() => setDraftAmt(Math.max(0, splitRemaining).toFixed(2))} disabled={splitVerifying}
   343	                    className="pressable border-2 border-foreground bg-card px-3 font-extrabold text-xs tracking-widest disabled:opacity-50">REM</button>
   344	                  <button onClick={addTender} disabled={splitVerifying}
   345	                    className="pressable-primary bg-primary text-primary-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-4 font-extrabold text-sm tracking-widest flex items-center gap-1 disabled:opacity-50">
   346	                    <Plus size={16}/> ADD
   347	                  </button>
   348	                </div>
   349	                {splitVerifying && (
   350	                  <div className="mt-2 bg-warning text-warning-foreground px-2 py-1 text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-center flex items-center justify-center gap-1">
   351	                    <Loader2 size={12} className="animate-spin"/> Verifying digital payment — please wait
   352	                  </div>
   353	                )}
   354	              </div>
   355	
   356	              {/* Tender list with verification badges */}
   357	              {splitTenders.length > 0 && (
   358	                <div className="border-2 border-foreground mb-3">
   359	                  {splitTenders.map((t, idx) => (
   360	                    <div key={idx} className="border-b-2 border-foreground last:border-b-0">
   361	                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2">
   362	                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   363	                          {tenderBadge(t)}
   364	                          <span className="font-extrabold text-sm uppercase tracking-wider">{t.method}</span>
   365	                          {isDigital(t.method) && t.bpStep === "success" && (
   366	                            <span className="text-[9px] font-mono text-muted-foreground">{t.bpTxnId.slice(0,10)}</span>
   367	                          )}
   368	                        </div>
   369	                        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
   370	                          <span className="font-mono font-extrabold tabular-nums">{formatINR(t.amount)}</span>
   371	                          <button onClick={() => removeSplitTender(idx)}
   372	                            disabled={activeSplitIdx === idx}
   373	                            className="border-2 border-foreground p-1 hover:bg-destructive hover:text-destructive-foreground disabled:opacity-30">
   374	                            <Trash2 size={14}/>
   375	                          </button>
   376	                        </div>
   377	                      </div>
   378	                      {/* Inline BharatPe panel for the actively-verifying tender */}
   379	                      {activeSplitIdx === idx && renderBPPanel(t.method, t.bpStep, t.bpQR, t.bpTxnId, t.amount,
   380	                        () => {
   381	                          splitPollCancelRef.current = true;
   382	                          setActiveSplitIdx(null);
   383	                          setSplitTenders((prev) => prev.map((x, i) => i === idx ? { ...x, bpStep: "idle" } : x));
   384	                        }
   385	                      )}
   386	                    </div>
   387	                  ))}
   388	                </div>
   389	              )}
   390	
   391	              {hasUnverifiedDigital && splitTenders.length > 0 && !splitVerifying && (
   392	                <div className="bg-warning text-warning-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-3 py-2 mb-3 text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-center">
   393	                  Digital payments pending verification
   394	                </div>
   395	              )}
   396	            </>
   397	          )}
   398	
   399	          {error && (
   400	            <div className="bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground font-extrabold text-center py-2 mb-3 text-sm uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
   401	              <WifiOff size={16}/> {error}
   402	            </div>
   403	          )}
   404	
   405	          <div className="border-2 border-foreground">
   406	            <div className="flex justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b-2 border-foreground bg-secondary">
   407	              <span className="font-extrabold uppercase text-sm tracking-wider">Subtotal {pride && <span className="text-accent">· PRIDE</span>}</span>
   408	              <span className="font-mono font-extrabold text-lg tabular-nums">{formatINR(subtotal)}</span>
   409	            </div>
   410	            {(split ? splitSurcharge : singleSurcharge) > 0 && (
   411	              <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b-2 border-foreground bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground">
   412	                <span className="font-extrabold uppercase text-sm tracking-wider flex items-center gap-2">
   413	                  <AlertTriangle size={16}/> Sodexo Surcharge (+5%)
   414	                </span>
   415	                <span className="font-mono font-extrabold text-lg tabular-nums">+{formatINR(split ? splitSurcharge : singleSurcharge)}</span>
   416	              </div>
   417	            )}
   418	            <div className="flex items-end justify-between px-4 py-3 bg-foreground text-background">
   419	              <span className="font-extrabold uppercase text-sm tracking-widest">{split ? "Due" : "Total"}</span>
   420	              <span className="font-mono font-extrabold tabular-nums leading-none" style={{ fontSize: 36 }}>
   421	                {formatINR(split ? splitTotalDue : singleTotal)}
   422	              </span>
   423	            </div>
   424	            {split && (
   425	              <div className={`flex items-end justify-between px-4 py-2 border-t-2 border-foreground
   426	                ${Math.abs(splitRemaining)<0.01 && !hasUnverifiedDigital ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground" : "bg-warning text-warning-foreground"}`}>
   427	                <span className="font-extrabold uppercase text-sm tracking-widest">
   428	                  {splitRemaining > 0.01 ? "Remaining" : splitRemaining < -0.01 ? "Overpaid"
   429	                    : hasUnverifiedDigital ? "Verifying..." : "Balanced ✓"}
   430	                </span>
   431	                <span className="font-mono font-extrabold tabular-nums text-2xl">{formatINR(Math.abs(splitRemaining))}</span>
   432	              </div>
   433	            )}
   434	          </div>
   435	
   436	          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 mt-5">
   437	            <button onClick={() => { resetBP(); splitPollCancelRef.current = true; setStage("pos"); }}
   438	              className="pressable border-2 border-foreground bg-card h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest">CANCEL</button>
   439	            <button onClick={confirm} disabled={!canConfirm}
   440	              className="pressable-primary bg-primary text-primary-foreground border-2 border-foreground h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest text-lg disabled:bg-muted disabled:text-muted-foreground disabled:shadow-none disabled:cursor-not-allowed flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
   441	              {loading ? (
   442	                <><Loader2 size={20} className="animate-spin"/> PROCESSING...</>
   443	              ) : (
   444	                <>CONFIRM · {formatINR(split ? splitTotalDue : singleTotal)}</>
   445	              )}
   446	            </button>
   447	          </div>
   448	        </div>
   449	      </div>
   450	    </div>
   451	  );
   452	}

   160	                    : <Square size={20} className="text-muted-foreground" />}
   161	                </div>
   162	                <div className="col-span-5">
   163	                  <div className="font-extrabold text-sm leading-tight">{item.name}</div>
   164	                  <div className="font-mono text-[10px] font-bold text-muted-foreground">
   165	                    {item.pid} · {formatINR(item.unitPrice)}{item.weighed ? "/KG" : ""}
   166	                  </div>
   167	                </div>
   168	                <div className="col-span-2 text-center font-mono font-extrabold text-sm tabular-nums">
   169	                  {item.weighed ? item.originalQty.toFixed(2) : item.originalQty}
   170	                </div>
   171	                <div className="col-span-2 flex items-center justify-center gap-1" onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
   172	                  {item.selected ? (
   173	                    <>
   174	                      <button onClick={() => setReturnQty(item.pid, +(item.returnQty - (item.weighed ? 0.1 : 1)).toFixed(3))}
   175	                        className="border-2 border-foreground w-6 h-6 font-extrabold text-sm hover:bg-foreground hover:text-background">−</button>
   176	                      <span className="font-mono font-extrabold text-sm w-10 text-center tabular-nums">
   177	                        {item.weighed ? item.returnQty.toFixed(2) : item.returnQty}
   178	                      </span>
   179	                      <button onClick={() => setReturnQty(item.pid, +(item.returnQty + (item.weighed ? 0.1 : 1)).toFixed(3))}
   180	                        className="border-2 border-foreground w-6 h-6 font-extrabold text-sm hover:bg-foreground hover:text-background">+</button>
   181	                    </>
   182	                  ) : (
   183	                    <span className="font-mono text-sm text-muted-foreground">—</span>
   184	                  )}
   185	                </div>
   186	                <div className="col-span-2 text-right font-mono font-extrabold text-sm tabular-nums">
   187	                  {item.selected ? formatINR(item.unitPrice * item.returnQty) : "—"}
   188	                </div>
   189	              </div>
   190	            ))}
   191	          </div>
   192	
   193	          {/* Refund method */}
   194	          <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">Refund Payout Method</div>
   195	          <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 mb-4">
   196	            {([
   197	              { m: "Cash" as PaymentMethod, icon: Banknote, label: "CASH" },
   198	              { m: "UPI" as PaymentMethod, icon: Smartphone, label: "UPI" },
   199	              { m: "Card" as PaymentMethod, icon: CreditCard, label: "CARD" },
   200	            ]).map(({ m, icon: Icon, label }) => (
   201	              <button key={m} onClick={() => setRefundMethod(m)}
   202	                className={`pressable border-2 border-foreground h-14 font-extrabold text-xs tracking-widest flex items-center justify-center gap-2
   203	                  ${refundMethod === m ? "bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground" : "bg-card hover:bg-secondary"}`}>
   204	                <Icon size={20} /> {label}
   205	              </button>
   206	            ))}
   207	          </div>
   208	          {lookedUpTx.method !== refundMethod && (
   209	            <div className="bg-warning text-warning-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-3 py-2 mb-4 flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">
   210	              <AlertTriangle size={14} />
   211	              Original payment was {lookedUpTx.method} · Refunding as {refundMethod}
   212	            </div>
   213	          )}
   214	
   215	          {returnError && (
   216	            <div className="bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground font-extrabold text-center py-2 mb-3 text-sm uppercase tracking-wider border-2 border-foreground">
   217	              {returnError}
   218	            </div>
   219	          )}
   220	
   221	          {/* Refund total */}
   222	          <div className="border-2 border-foreground mb-4">
   223	            <div className="flex items-end justify-between px-4 py-3 bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground">
   224	              <div>
   225	                <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest">Refund Total</div>
   226	                <div className="text-[10px] font-bold opacity-80">
   227	                  {selectedItems.length} item{selectedItems.length !== 1 && "s"} · {refundMethod}
   228	                </div>
   229	              </div>
   230	              <div className="font-mono font-extrabold tabular-nums leading-none" style={{ fontSize: 36 }}>
   231	                −{formatINR(refundTotal)}
   232	              </div>
   233	            </div>
   234	          </div>
   235	
   236	          {/* Action buttons */}
   237	          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
   238	            <button onClick={clearReturn}
   239	              className="pressable border-2 border-foreground bg-card h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest">
   240	              CANCEL
   241	            </button>
   242	            <button onClick={() => setShowPin(true)}
   243	              disabled={!canProcess || returnLoading}
   244	              className="pressable-primary bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground border-2 border-foreground h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest text-base flex items-center justify-center gap-2 disabled:bg-muted disabled:text-muted-foreground disabled:shadow-none disabled:cursor-not-allowed">
   245	              <RotateCcw size={20} /> PROCESS REFUND
   246	            </button>
   247	          </div>
   248	        </div>
   249	      </div>
   250	
   251	      {/* Manager PIN auth overlay */}
   252	      {showPin && (
   253	        <ManagerPinModal
   254	          onSubmit={handleRefund}
   255	          onClose={() => setShowPin(false)}
   256	          loading={returnLoading}
   257	          error={returnError}
   258	        />
   259	      )}
   260	    </div>
   261	  );
   262	}


</details>

<details><summary>Tool Result: ReadFile (`packages/freshon-api/src/client.ts`)</summary>

<!-- call_id: ReadFile:10 -->
<system>197 lines read from file starting from line 1. Total lines in file: 197. End of file reached.</system>
     1	// packages/freshon-api/src/client.ts
     2	// Central Axios HTTP client for all FreshOn apps.
     3	// Handles JWT Bearer auth via localStorage (for mobile/Tauri) with automatic
     4	// silent refresh and request queuing during refresh.
     5	
     6	import axios, {
     7	  AxiosInstance,
     8	  AxiosError,
     9	  InternalAxiosRequestConfig,
    10	} from "axios";
    11	
    12	// ─── Token Storage ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    13	
    14	const ACCESS_KEY = "freshon_access_token";
    15	const REFRESH_KEY = "freshon_refresh_token";
    16	
    17	export function setAuthTokens(access: string, refresh: string): void {
    18	  localStorage.setItem(ACCESS_KEY, access);
    19	  localStorage.setItem(REFRESH_KEY, refresh);
    20	}
    21	
    22	export function getAccessToken(): string | null {
    23	  return localStorage.getItem(ACCESS_KEY);
    24	}
    25	
    26	export function getRefreshToken(): string | null {
    27	  return localStorage.getItem(REFRESH_KEY);
    28	}
    29	
    30	export function clearAuthTokens(): void {
    31	  localStorage.removeItem(ACCESS_KEY);
    32	  localStorage.removeItem(REFRESH_KEY);
    33	}
    34	
    35	// ─── Configuration ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    36	
    37	export interface FreshOnClientConfig {
    38	  /** Base URL for the Django backend (e.g. "https://yogesh843120.pythonanywhere.com") */
    39	  baseURL: string;
    40	  /** Path to redirect to on auth failure (default: "/welcome") */
    41	  authRedirectPath?: string;
    42	  /** Public endpoints that skip the Bearer header (default: register, login, refresh) */
    43	  publicEndpoints?: string[];
    44	}
    45	
    46	const DEFAULT_PUBLIC_ENDPOINTS = [
    47	  "/api/auth/register/",
    48	  "/api/auth/login/",
    49	  "/api/auth/token/refresh/",
    50	];
    51	
    52	// ─── Client Factory ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    53	
    54	let _instance: AxiosInstance | null = null;
    55	let _config: FreshOnClientConfig | null = null;
    56	
    57	/**
    58	 * Initialize the FreshOn API client. Must be called once at app startup
    59	 * (e.g. in main.tsx or App.tsx) before any API module is used.
    60	 *
    61	 * ```ts
    62	 * import { initClient } from "@freshon/api";
    63	 * initClient({ baseURL: import.meta.env.VITE_API_MAIN_URL });
    64	 * ```
    65	 */
    66	export function initClient(config: FreshOnClientConfig): AxiosInstance {
    67	  _config = config;
    68	
    69	  const client = axios.create({
    70	    baseURL: config.baseURL,
    71	    withCredentials: true,
    72	    xsrfCookieName: "csrftoken",
    73	    xsrfHeaderName: "X-CSRFToken",
    74	  });
    75	
    76	  // ── Request interceptor: attach Bearer token ──────────────────────
    77	
    78	  const publicEndpoints = config.publicEndpoints ?? DEFAULT_PUBLIC_ENDPOINTS;
    79	
    80	  client.interceptors.request.use((req: InternalAxiosRequestConfig) => {
    81	    const isPublic = publicEndpoints.some((ep) => req.url?.includes(ep));
    82	
    83	    if (!isPublic) {
    84	      const token = getAccessToken();
    85	      if (token) {
    86	        req.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
    87	      }
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    return req;
    91	  });
    92	
    93	  // ── Response interceptor: silent refresh on 401 ───────────────────
    94	
    95	  let isRefreshing = false;
    96	  let refreshSubscribers: Array<() => void> = [];
    97	
    98	  function onRefreshed() {
    99	    refreshSubscribers.forEach((cb) => cb());
   100	    refreshSubscribers = [];
   101	  }
   102	
   103	  function redirectToAuth() {
   104	    clearAuthTokens();
   105	    if (typeof window !== "undefined") {
   106	      window.location.href = config.authRedirectPath ?? "/welcome";
   107	    }
   108	  }
   109	
   110	  client.interceptors.response.use(
   111	    (response) => response,
   112	    async (error: AxiosError) => {
   113	      const originalRequest = error.config as InternalAxiosRequestConfig & {
   114	        _retry?: boolean;
   115	      };
   116	
   117	      if (
   118	        error.response?.status === 401 &&
   119	        originalRequest &&
   120	        !originalRequest._retry &&
   121	        !originalRequest.url?.includes("/api/auth/token/refresh/")
   122	      ) {
   123	        originalRequest._retry = true;
   124	
   125	        // Queue subsequent requests while refresh is in progress
   126	        if (isRefreshing) {
   127	          return new Promise<void>((resolve) => {
   128	            refreshSubscribers.push(resolve);
   129	          }).then(() => client(originalRequest));
   130	        }
   131	
   132	        const refreshToken = getRefreshToken();
   133	        if (!refreshToken) {
   134	          redirectToAuth();
   135	          return Promise.reject(error);
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        isRefreshing = true;
   139	
   140	        try {
   141	          const refreshResponse = await axios.post(
   142	            `${config.baseURL}/api/auth/token/refresh/`,
   143	            { refresh: refreshToken },
   144	            { withCredentials: true }
   145	          );
   146	
   147	          const { access, refresh } = refreshResponse.data ?? {};
   148	
   149	          if (!access || !refresh) {
   150	            throw new Error("Refresh response missing tokens");
   151	          }
   152	
   153	          setAuthTokens(access, refresh);
   154	          isRefreshing = false;
   155	          onRefreshed();
   156	
   157	          return client(originalRequest);
   158	        } catch {
   159	          isRefreshing = false;
   160	          refreshSubscribers = [];
   161	          redirectToAuth();
   162	          return Promise.reject(error);
   163	        }
   164	      }
   165	
   166	      return Promise.reject(error);
   167	    }
   168	  );
   169	
   170	  _instance = client;
   171	  return client;
   172	}
   173	
   174	/**
   175	 * Returns the initialized Axios instance.
   176	 * Throws if `initClient` was not called first.
   177	 */
   178	export function getClient(): AxiosInstance {
   179	  if (!_instance) {
   180	    throw new Error(
   181	      "[@freshon/api] Client not initialized. Call initClient({ baseURL }) before using API modules."
   182	    );
   183	  }
   184	  return _instance;
   185	}
   186	
   187	/**
   188	 * Returns the client config (baseURL etc.) for use in WebSocket connections.
   189	 */
   190	export function getClientConfig(): FreshOnClientConfig {
   191	  if (!_config) {
   192	    throw new Error(
   193	      "[@freshon/api] Client not initialized. Call initClient({ baseURL }) first."
   194	    );
   195	  }
   196	  return _config;
   197	}

  try {

    return txs.map((tx) => ({
      id: tx.id,
      customerId: String(tx.customer_id),

        name: i.name,
        unitPrice: Number(i.unit_price),
        weighed: i.weighed,

      })),

      surcharge: Number(tx.surcharge),
      total: Number(tx.total),
      timestamp: tx.timestamp || Date.now(),
      receiptDelivery: tx.receipt_delivery,
    }));
  } catch {

},

    91	      setBpQR(qr.qr_string); setBpTxnId(qr.transaction_id);

    93	      const result = await pollUntilResolved(qr.transaction_id, (s) => {

   329	                <Btn m="Cash" label="CASH" active={method==="Cash"} onClick={() => handleMethodChange("Cash")}/>
   330	                <Btn m="UPI" label="UPI" active={method==="UPI"} onClick={() => handleMethodChange("UPI")}/>
   331	                <Btn m="Card" label="CARD" active={method==="Card"} onClick={() => handleMethodChange("Card")}/>
   332	                <Btn m="Sodexo" label="SODEXO" special active={method==="Sodexo"} onClick={() => handleMethodChange("Sodexo")}/>
   333	                <Btn m="Wallet" label={`WALLET${customer?.wallet_balance !== undefined ? `\n(Bal: ${formatINR(customer.wallet_balance)})` : ""}`} active={method==="Wallet"} onClick={() => handleMethodChange("Wallet")}
   334	                  disabled={!customer || (customer?.wallet_balance ?? 0) <= 0}/>
   335	              </div>
   336	              {method === "Wallet" && customer && (customer.wallet_balance ?? 0) < singleTotal && (
   337	                <div className="bg-warning text-warning-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-3 py-2 mb-3 text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-center flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
   338	                  <AlertTriangle size={14}/> Low Wallet Balance · {formatINR(customer.wallet_balance ?? 0)} available
   339	                </div>
   340	              )}
   341	              {isDigital(method) && renderBPPanel(method, bpStep, bpQR, bpTxnId, singleTotal, resetBP)}
   342	            </>
   343	          ) : (
   344	            <>
   345	              <div className="text-[11px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">Split Tenders</div>
   346	              <div className="border-2 border-foreground bg-background p-3 mb-3">
   347	                <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mb-3">
   348	                  {(["Cash","UPI","Card","Sodexo","Wallet"] as PaymentMethod[]).map((m) => (
   349	                    <Btn key={m} m={m} label={m.toUpperCase()} special={m==="Sodexo"} active={draftMethod===m}
   350	                      disabled={splitVerifying} onClick={() => setDraftMethod(m)}/>
   351	                  ))}
   352	                </div>
   353	                <div className="flex gap-2">
   354	                  <input type="number" inputMode="decimal" value={draftAmt}
   355	                    onChange={(e) => setDraftAmt(e.target.value)} disabled={splitVerifying}
   356	                    placeholder={`AMOUNT (REMAINING ${formatINR(Math.max(0, splitRemaining))})`}
   357	                    className="flex-1 border-2 border-foreground bg-background px-3 py-2 font-mono font-bold text-base outline-none focus:border-primary disabled:opacity-50"/>
   358	                  <button onClick={() => setDraftAmt(Math.max(0, splitRemaining).toFixed(2))} disabled={splitVerifying}
   359	                    className="pressable border-2 border-foreground bg-card px-3 font-extrabold text-xs tracking-widest disabled:opacity-50">REM</button>
   360	                  <button onClick={addTender} disabled={splitVerifying}
   361	                    className="pressable-primary bg-primary text-primary-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-4 font-extrabold text-sm tracking-widest flex items-center gap-1 disabled:opacity-50">
   362	                    <Plus size={16}/> ADD
   363	                  </button>
   364	                </div>
   365	                {splitVerifying && (
   366	                  <div className="mt-2 bg-warning text-warning-foreground px-2 py-1 text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-center flex items-center justify-center gap-1">
   367	                    <Loader2 size={12} className="animate-spin"/> Verifying digital payment — please wait
   368	                  </div>
   369	                )}
   370	              </div>
   371	
   372	              {/* Tender list with verification badges */}
   373	              {splitTenders.length > 0 && (
   374	                <div className="border-2 border-foreground mb-3">
   375	                  {splitTenders.map((t, idx) => (
   376	                    <div key={idx} className="border-b-2 border-foreground last:border-b-0">
   377	                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2">
   378	                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   379	                          {tenderBadge(t)}
   380	                          <span className="font-extrabold text-sm uppercase tracking-wider">{t.method}</span>
   381	                          {isDigital(t.method) && t.bpStep === "success" && (
   382	                            <span className="text-[9px] font-mono text-muted-foreground">{t.bpTxnId.slice(0,10)}</span>
   383	                          )}
   384	                        </div>
   385	                        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
   386	                          <span className="font-mono font-extrabold tabular-nums">{formatINR(t.amount)}</span>
   387	                          <button onClick={() => removeSplitTender(idx)}
   388	                            disabled={activeSplitIdx === idx}
   389	                            className="border-2 border-foreground p-1 hover:bg-destructive hover:text-destructive-foreground disabled:opacity-30">
   390	                            <Trash2 size={14}/>
   391	                          </button>
   392	                        </div>
   393	                      </div>
   394	                      {/* Inline BharatPe panel for the actively-verifying tender */}
   395	                      {activeSplitIdx === idx && renderBPPanel(t.method, t.bpStep, t.bpQR, t.bpTxnId, t.amount,
   396	                        () => {
   397	                          splitPollCancelRef.current = true;
   398	                          setActiveSplitIdx(null);
   399	                          setSplitTenders((prev) => prev.map((x, i) => i === idx ? { ...x, bpStep: "idle" } : x));
   400	                        }
   401	                      )}
   402	                    </div>
   403	                  ))}
   404	                </div>
   405	              )}
   406	
   407	              {hasUnverifiedDigital && splitTenders.length > 0 && !splitVerifying && (
   408	                <div className="bg-warning text-warning-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-3 py-2 mb-3 text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-center">
   409	                  Digital payments pending verification
   410	                </div>
   411	              )}
   412	            </>
   413	          )}
   414	
   415	          {error && (
   416	            <div className="bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground font-extrabold text-center py-2 mb-3 text-sm uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
   417	              <WifiOff size={16}/> {error}
   418	            </div>
   419	          )}
   420	
   421	          <div className="border-2 border-foreground">
   422	            <div className="flex justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b-2 border-foreground bg-secondary">
   423	              <span className="font-extrabold uppercase text-sm tracking-wider">Subtotal {pride && <span className="text-accent">· PRIDE</span>}</span>
   424	              <span className="font-mono font-extrabold text-lg tabular-nums">{formatINR(subtotal)}</span>
   425	            </div>
   426	            {(split ? splitSurcharge : singleSurcharge) > 0 && (
   427	              <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b-2 border-foreground bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground">
   428	                <span className="font-extrabold uppercase text-sm tracking-wider flex items-center gap-2">
   429	                  <AlertTriangle size={16}/> Sodexo Surcharge (+5%)
   430	                </span>
   431	                <span className="font-mono font-extrabold text-lg tabular-nums">+{formatINR(split ? splitSurcharge : singleSurcharge)}</span>
   432	              </div>
   433	            )}
   434	            <div className="flex items-end justify-between px-4 py-3 bg-foreground text-background">
   435	              <span className="font-extrabold uppercase text-sm tracking-widest">{split ? "Due" : "Total"}</span>
   436	              <span className="font-mono font-extrabold tabular-nums leading-none" style={{ fontSize: 36 }}>
   437	                {formatINR(split ? splitTotalDue : singleTotal)}
   438	              </span>
   439	            </div>
   440	            {split && (
   441	              <div className={`flex items-end justify-between px-4 py-2 border-t-2 border-foreground
   442	                ${Math.abs(splitRemaining)<0.01 && !hasUnverifiedDigital ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground" : "bg-warning text-warning-foreground"}`}>
   443	                <span className="font-extrabold uppercase text-sm tracking-widest">
   444	                  {splitRemaining > 0.01 ? "Remaining" : splitRemaining < -0.01 ? "Overpaid"
   445	                    : hasUnverifiedDigital ? "Verifying..." : "Balanced ✓"}
   446	                </span>
   447	                <span className="font-mono font-extrabold tabular-nums text-2xl">{formatINR(Math.abs(splitRemaining))}</span>
   448	              </div>
   449	            )}
   450	          </div>
   451	
   452	          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 mt-5">
   453	            <button onClick={() => { resetBP(); splitPollCancelRef.current = true; setStage("pos"); }}
   454	              className="pressable border-2 border-foreground bg-card h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest">CANCEL</button>
   455	            <button onClick={confirm} disabled={!canConfirm}
   456	              className="pressable-primary bg-primary text-primary-foreground border-2 border-foreground h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest text-lg disabled:bg-muted disabled:text-muted-foreground disabled:shadow-none disabled:cursor-not-allowed flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
   457	              {loading ? (
   458	                <><Loader2 size={20} className="animate-spin"/> PROCESSING...</>
   459	              ) : (
   460	                <>CONFIRM · {formatINR(split ? splitTotalDue : singleTotal)}</>
   461	              )}
   462	            </button>
   463	          </div>
   464	        </div>
   465	      </div>
   466	    </div>
   467	  );
   468	}


</details>
