   308	                <div className="col-span-2 text-center font-mono font-extrabold text-sm tabular-nums">
   309	                  {item.weighed ? item.originalQty.toFixed(2) : item.originalQty}
   310	                </div>
   311	                <div className="col-span-2 flex items-center justify-center gap-1" onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
   312	                  {item.selected ? (
   313	                    <>
   314	                      <button onClick={() => setReturnQty(item.pid, +(item.returnQty - (item.weighed ? 0.1 : 1)).toFixed(3))}
   315	                        className="border-2 border-foreground w-6 h-6 font-extrabold text-sm hover:bg-foreground hover:text-background">−</button>
   316	                      <span className="font-mono font-extrabold text-sm w-10 text-center tabular-nums">
   317	                        {item.weighed ? item.returnQty.toFixed(2) : item.returnQty}
   318	                      </span>
   319	                      <button onClick={() => setReturnQty(item.pid, +(item.returnQty + (item.weighed ? 0.1 : 1)).toFixed(3))}
   320	                        className="border-2 border-foreground w-6 h-6 font-extrabold text-sm hover:bg-foreground hover:text-background">+</button>
   321	                    </>
   322	                  ) : (
   323	                    <span className="font-mono text-sm text-muted-foreground">—</span>
   324	                  )}
   325	                </div>
   326	                <div className="col-span-2 text-right font-mono font-extrabold text-sm tabular-nums">
   327	                  {item.selected ? formatINR(item.unitPrice * item.returnQty) : "—"}
   328	                </div>
   329	              </div>
   330	            ))}
   331	          </div>
   332	
   333	          {/* Refund method */}
   334	          <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">Refund Payout Method</div>
   335	          <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mb-4">
   336	            {([
   337	              { m: "Cash" as PaymentMethod, icon: Banknote, label: "CASH" },
   338	              { m: "UPI" as PaymentMethod, icon: Smartphone, label: "UPI" },
   339	              { m: "Card" as PaymentMethod, icon: CreditCard, label: "CARD" },
   340	              { m: "Wallet" as PaymentMethod, icon: Wallet, label: "WALLET" },
   341	            ]).map(({ m, icon: Icon, label }) => (
   342	              <button key={m} onClick={() => setRefundMethod(m)}
   343	                className={`pressable border-2 border-foreground h-14 font-extrabold text-xs tracking-widest flex items-center justify-center gap-2
   344	                  ${refundMethod === m ? "bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground" : "bg-card hover:bg-secondary"}`}>
   345	                <Icon size={20} /> {label}
   346	              </button>
   347	            ))}
   348	          </div>
   349	          {lookedUpTx.method !== refundMethod && (
   350	            <div className="bg-warning text-warning-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-3 py-2 mb-4 flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">
   351	              <AlertTriangle size={14} />
   352	              Original payment was {lookedUpTx.method} · Refunding as {refundMethod}
   353	            </div>
   354	          )}
   355	
   356	          {returnError && (
   357	            <div className="bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground font-extrabold text-center py-2 mb-3 text-sm uppercase tracking-wider border-2 border-foreground">
   358	              {returnError}
   359	            </div>
   360	          )}
   361	
   362	          {/* Refund total */}
   363	          <div className="border-2 border-foreground mb-4">
   364	            <div className="flex items-end justify-between px-4 py-3 bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground">
   365	              <div>
   366	                <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest">Refund Total</div>
   367	                <div className="text-[10px] font-bold opacity-80">
   368	                  {selectedItems.length} item{selectedItems.length !== 1 && "s"} · {refundMethod}
   369	                </div>
   370	              </div>
   371	              <div className="font-mono font-extrabold tabular-nums leading-none" style={{ fontSize: 36 }}>
   372	                −{formatINR(refundTotal)}
   373	              </div>
   374	            </div>
   375	          </div>
   376	
   377	          {/* Action buttons */}
   378	          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
   379	            <button onClick={clearReturn}
   380	              className="pressable border-2 border-foreground bg-card h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest">
   381	              CANCEL
   382	            </button>
   383	            <button onClick={() => setShowPin(true)}
   384	              disabled={!canProcess || returnLoading}
   385	              className="pressable-primary bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground border-2 border-foreground h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest text-base flex items-center justify-center gap-2 disabled:bg-muted disabled:text-muted-foreground disabled:shadow-none disabled:cursor-not-allowed">
   386	              <RotateCcw size={20} /> PROCESS REFUND
   387	            </button>
   388	          </div>
   389	        </div>
   390	      </div>

   395	          onSubmit={handleRefund}
   396	          onClose={() => setShowPin(false)}
   397	          loading={returnLoading}
   398	          error={returnError}

All tasks are complete. Here's a summary of the changes:

**1. Types (`packages/freshon-api/src/types.ts`)**
- Already contained `"Wallet"` in `PosPaymentMethod` and `wallet_balance?: number` in `PosCustomer` — no changes needed.

**2. API SDK (`packages/freshon-api/src/modules/pos.ts`)**
- Added `fetchCustomerTransactions(phone: string)` → calls `GET /api/pos/customers/transactions/?phone=...` and returns `PosTransaction[]`.

**3. POS Store (`Fpos/src/pos/store.ts`)**
- Added `"Wallet"` to the local `PaymentMethod` type.
- Added `fetchCustomerTransactions` action (maps backend `PosTransaction[]` to local `Transaction[]`).
- Updated `pay`: after a successful order, if any tender is `"Wallet"`, deducts the wallet amount from `selectedCustomer.wallet_balance`.
- Updated `processRefund`: after a successful refund, if `refundMethod === "Wallet"`, credits the refund amount back to `selectedCustomer.wallet_balance`.

**4. Wallet Checkout (`Fpos/src/pos/components/PaymentDrawer.tsx`)**
- Added `Wallet` button to the method grid (5-column layout) showing live balance: `(Bal: ₹500)`.
- Wallet button is disabled when no customer is selected or balance is ≤ 0.
- Shows **"Low Wallet Balance"** warning banner when Wallet is selected and `total > wallet_balance`.
- Blocks confirmation when Wallet is selected with insufficient balance.
- Auto-defaults payment method to **Wallet** on drawer open if the customer is a **PRIDE** member with a positive balance.
- Added Wallet to split-tender options.

**5. No-Receipt Returns (`Fpos/src/pos/components/ReturnScreen.tsx`)**
- Added **Phone Number** search bar in the lookup phase (alongside existing Receipt ID search).
- On finding a customer, displays their **Last 5 Transactions** in a high-contrast table (Receipt ID, Date, Amount).
- Clicking a transaction loads it into the return view via `lookupTransaction(tx.id)`.
- Changed default **Refund Method** from `"Cash"` to `"Wallet"`.
- Added **Wallet** as a refund payout option alongside Cash, UPI, and Card.

**Build verification:** `vite build` passes cleanly with zero errors.

## 4. Physical Cash Drawer Pulse
- **Goal**: Physically pop the drawer on Cash sales.
- **Action**: Update `open_cash_drawer` in `lib.rs` to send the raw ESC/POS byte sequence `[27, 112, 0, 25, 250]` to the default printer.

   600	    }
   601	  },
   602	
   603	  // ── Stage & Payment ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   604	
   605	  setStage: (s) => set({ stage: s }),
   606	
   607	  pay: async (tenders, bharatpeTxnId) => {
   608	    const { cart, selectedCustomer, shift } = get();
   609	    if (!selectedCustomer || cart.length === 0 || tenders.length === 0)
   610	      return null;
   611	
   612	    const pride = !!selectedCustomer.pride;
   613	    const subtotal = +subtotalOf(cart, pride).toFixed(2);
   614	    const gross = +grossSubtotalOf(cart).toFixed(2);
   615	    const memberDiscount = +(gross - subtotal).toFixed(2);
   616	
   617	    const sodexoTender = tenders.find((t) => t.method === "Sodexo");
   618	    const surchargeSimple = sodexoTender
   619	      ? +(sodexoTender.amount * 0.05).toFixed(2)
   620	      : 0;
   621	    const total = +(subtotal + surchargeSimple).toFixed(2);
   622	    const cashAmt = tenders
   623	      .filter((t) => t.method === "Cash")
   624	      .reduce((s, t) => s + t.amount, 0);
   625	    const isSplit = tenders.length > 1;
   626	    const method = isSplit ? ("Split" as const) : tenders[0].method;
   627	    const walletAmt = tenders
   628	      .filter((t) => t.method === "Wallet")
   629	      .reduce((s, t) => s + t.amount, 0);
   630	    set({ loading: true, error: null });
   631	
   632	    try {
   633	      // Map cart items to SDK format (snake_case)
   634	      const sdkItems = cart.map((i) => ({
   635	        pid: i.pid,
   636	        name: i.name,
   637	        unit_price: memberPriceOf(i, pride),
   638	        weighed: i.weighed,
   639	        quantity: i.quantity,
   640	        member_eligible: i.memberEligible,
   641	      }));
   642	
   643	      const sdkTenders = tenders.map((t) => ({
   644	        method: t.method,
   645	        amount: t.amount,
   646	      }));
   647	
   648	      // Submit to backend
   649	      const backendTx = await pos.createOrder({
   650	        customer_id: String(selectedCustomer.id),
   651	        items: sdkItems,
   652	        tenders: sdkTenders,
   653	        subtotal,
   654	        member_discount: memberDiscount,
   655	        surcharge: surchargeSimple,
   656	        total,
   657	      });
   658	
   659	      // Build local transaction from backend response
   660	      const tx: Transaction = {
   661	        id: backendTx.id,
   662	        customerId: String(selectedCustomer.id),
   663	        items: cart,
   664	        tenders,
   665	        method,
   666	        subtotal,
   667	        memberDiscount,
   668	        surcharge: surchargeSimple,
   669	        total,
   670	        timestamp: backendTx.timestamp || Date.now(),
   671	        receiptDelivery: "Print",
   672	        bharatpeTxnId,
   673	      };
   674	
   675	      set((s) => ({
   676	        lastTransaction: tx,
   677	        stage: "receipt" as const,
   678	        loading: false,
   679	        selectedCustomer:
   680	          s.selectedCustomer && walletAmt > 0
   681	            ? {
   682	                ...s.selectedCustomer,
   683	                wallet_balance: +((s.selectedCustomer.wallet_balance ?? 0) - walletAmt).toFixed(2),
   684	              }
   685	            : s.selectedCustomer,
   686	        shift: s.shift
   687	          ? {
   688	              ...s.shift,
   689	              cashSales: +(s.shift.cashSales + cashAmt).toFixed(2),
   690	              totalSales: +(s.shift.totalSales + total).toFixed(2),
   691	              txnCount: s.shift.txnCount + 1,
   692	            }
   693	          : s.shift,
   694	        products: s.products.map((p) => {
   695	          const ci = cart.find((c) => c.pid === p.pid);
   696	          return ci
   697	            ? { ...p, stock: Math.max(0, +(p.stock - ci.quantity).toFixed(3)) }
   698	            : p;
   699	        }),
   700	      }));
   701	
   702	      return tx;
   703	    } catch (err: any) {
   704	      const message =
   705	        err?.response?.data?.error || err?.message || "Order submission failed";
   706	      set({ error: message, loading: false });
   707	      return null;
   708	    }
   709	  },

   711	    set((s) => ({
   712	      lastTransaction: s.lastTransaction
   713	        ? { ...s.lastTransaction, receiptDelivery: d }
   714	        : null,
   715	    })),

    66	      const customer = results[0];
    67	      setFoundCustomer({
    68	        id: customer.id,
    69	        name: customer.name,
    70	        phone: customer.phone,
    71	        wallet_balance: customer.wallet_balance,
    72	      });
    73	      selectCustomer(customer);
    74	      setTxLoading(true);
    75	      const txs = await fetchCustomerTransactions(phoneQuery.trim());
    76	      setCustomerTxs(txs.slice(0, 5));
    77	      setTxLoading(false);
    78	    } catch {
    79	      setPhoneSearchError("Search failed");
    80	    } finally {
    81	      setPhoneSearching(false);
    82	    }
    83	  };
    84	
    85	  const handleTxSelect = async (tx: Transaction) => {
    86	    setPhoneSearchError("");
    87	    const ok = await lookupTransaction(tx.id);
    88	    if (!ok && !returnError) setPhoneSearchError("Transaction not found");
    89	  };
    90	
    91	  const selectedItems = lookedUpTx?.items.filter((i) => i.selected) || [];
    92	  const refundTotal = selectedItems.reduce((s, i) => s + i.unitPrice * i.returnQty, 0);
    93	  const canProcess = selectedItems.length > 0 && refundTotal > 0;
    94	
    95	  const handleRefund = async (managerPin: string) => {
    96	    const ok = await processRefund(managerPin, refundMethod);
    97	    if (!ok) throw new Error("Refund failed"); // triggers shake in ManagerPinModal
    98	  };
    99	
   100	  // ── Search phase ──
   101	  if (!lookedUpTx) {
   102	    return (
   103	      <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-foreground/80 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
   104	        <div className="border-sharp-3 bg-card w-[580px]" style={{ boxShadow: "10px 10px 0 0 hsl(var(--foreground))" }}>
   105	          <div className="flex items-center justify-between bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground px-5 py-3 border-b-2 border-foreground">
   106	            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   107	              <RotateCcw size={22} />
   108	              <h2 className="text-xl font-extrabold uppercase tracking-tight">Return / Refund</h2>
   109	            </div>
   110	            <button onClick={clearReturn} className="border-2 border-destructive-foreground p-1 hover:bg-foreground">
   111	              <X size={18} />
   112	            </button>
   113	          </div>
   114	
   115	          <div className="p-5">
   116	            {/* Receipt ID Search */}
   117	            <label className="block text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">
   118	              Search Receipt ID
   119	            </label>
   120	            <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4">
   121	              <div className="flex items-center px-3 bg-foreground text-background border-2 border-foreground">
   122	                {returnLoading ? <Loader2 size={18} className="animate-spin" /> : <Search size={18} />}
   123	              </div>
   124	              <input
   125	                value={receiptId}
   126	                onChange={(e) => setReceiptId(e.target.value)}
   127	                onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && handleSearch()}
   128	                placeholder="PASTE OR TYPE RECEIPT UUID"
   129	                disabled={returnLoading}
   130	                className="flex-1 border-2 border-foreground bg-background px-3 py-2 font-mono font-bold text-base outline-none focus:border-primary disabled:opacity-50"
   131	              />
   132	              <button onClick={handleSearch} disabled={returnLoading}
   133	                className="pressable-primary bg-primary text-primary-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-5 font-extrabold text-sm tracking-widest disabled:opacity-50">
   134	                LOOK UP
   135	              </button>
   136	            </div>
   137	
   138	            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4">
   139	              <div className="flex-1 h-px bg-foreground/20"/>
   140	              <span className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">OR</span>
   141	              <div className="flex-1 h-px bg-foreground/20"/>
   142	            </div>
   143	
   144	            {/* Phone Search */}
   145	            <label className="block text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">
   146	              Search by Phone Number
   147	            </label>
   148	            <div className="flex gap-2 mb-3">
   149	              <div className="flex items-center px-3 bg-foreground text-background border-2 border-foreground">
   150	                {phoneSearching || txLoading ? <Loader2 size={18} className="animate-spin" /> : <Phone size={18} />}
   151	              </div>
   152	              <input
   153	                value={phoneQuery}
   154	                onChange={(e) => setPhoneQuery(e.target.value)}
   155	                onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && handlePhoneSearch()}
   156	                placeholder="ENTER CUSTOMER PHONE"
   157	                disabled={phoneSearching || txLoading}
   158	                className="flex-1 border-2 border-foreground bg-background px-3 py-2 font-mono font-bold text-base outline-none focus:border-primary disabled:opacity-50"
   159	              />
   160	              <button onClick={handlePhoneSearch} disabled={phoneSearching || txLoading}
   161	                className="pressable-primary bg-primary text-primary-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-5 font-extrabold text-sm tracking-widest disabled:opacity-50">
   162	                FIND
   163	              </button>
   164	            </div>
   165	
   166	            {(searchError || returnError || phoneSearchError) && (
   167	              <div className="bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground font-extrabold text-center py-2 text-sm uppercase tracking-wider border-2 border-foreground flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
   168	                <AlertTriangle size={16} /> {searchError || returnError || phoneSearchError}
   169	              </div>
   170	            )}
   171	
   172	            {/* Customer found + transaction history */}
   173	            {foundCustomer && (
   174	              <div className="mt-4">
   175	                <div className="border-2 border-foreground bg-background p-3 mb-3 flex items-center justify-between">
   176	                  <div>
   177	                    <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">Customer</div>
   178	                    <div className="font-extrabold text-sm">{foundCustomer.name}</div>
   179	                    <div className="font-mono text-[10px] font-bold text-muted-foreground">{foundCustomer.phone}</div>
   180	                  </div>
   181	                  <div className="text-right">
   182	                    <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">Wallet</div>
   183	                    <div className="font-mono font-extrabold text-sm tabular-nums">{formatINR(foundCustomer.wallet_balance ?? 0)}</div>
   184	                  </div>
   185	                </div>
   186	
   187	                <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">
   188	                  Last 5 Transactions
   189	                </div>
   190	                {txLoading ? (
   191	                  <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-6 text-muted-foreground">
   192	                    <Loader2 size={16} className="animate-spin" />
   193	                    <span className="font-extrabold text-xs uppercase tracking-widest">Loading history...</span>
   194	                  </div>
   195	                ) : customerTxs.length === 0 ? (
   196	                  <div className="border-2 border-foreground bg-background p-4 text-center text-muted-foreground font-extrabold text-xs uppercase tracking-widest">
   197	                    No transactions found
   198	                  </div>
   199	                ) : (
   200	                  <div className="border-2 border-foreground mb-3">
   201	                    <div className="grid grid-cols-12 px-3 py-2 bg-foreground text-background text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">
   202	                      <div className="col-span-4">Receipt ID</div>
   203	                      <div className="col-span-4 text-center">Date</div>
   204	                      <div className="col-span-3 text-right">Amount</div>
   205	                      <div className="col-span-1"></div>
   206	                    </div>
   207	                    {customerTxs.map((tx, idx) => (
   208	                      <button key={tx.id}
   209	                        onClick={() => handleTxSelect(tx)}
   210	                        className={`w-full grid grid-cols-12 px-3 py-2 items-center text-left border-b border-foreground/30 last:border-b-0 hover:bg-primary/10
   211	                          ${idx % 2 === 1 ? "bg-row-alt" : ""}`}>
   212	                        <div className="col-span-4 font-mono font-bold text-xs truncate">{tx.id.slice(0, 12).toUpperCase()}…</div>

   214	                        <div className="col-span-3 text-right font-mono font-extrabold text-sm tabular-nums">{formatINR(tx.total)}</div>
   215	                        <div className="col-span-1 text-right">
   216	                          <Search size={14} className="inline text-muted-foreground"/>
   217	                        </div>
   218	                      </button>
   219	                    ))}
   220	                  </div>
   221	                )}
   222	              </div>
   223	            )}
   224	
   225	            {!foundCustomer && (
   226	              <div className="mt-6 text-center text-muted-foreground">
   227	                <RotateCcw size={48} className="mx-auto mb-3 opacity-30" />
   228	                <div className="font-extrabold text-sm uppercase tracking-widest">Enter a Receipt ID or Phone to Begin</div>
   229	                <div className="text-xs font-bold mt-1">Find the ID on the printed receipt or search by customer phone</div>
   230	              </div>
   231	            )}
   232	          </div>
   233	        </div>
   234	      </div>
   235	    );
   236	  }
   237	
   238	  // ── Item selection phase ──
   239	  return (
   240	    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-foreground/80 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
   241	      <div className="border-sharp-3 bg-card w-[700px] max-h-[720px] overflow-y-auto scrollbar-sharp"
   242	        style={{ boxShadow: "10px 10px 0 0 hsl(var(--foreground))" }}>
   243	
   244	        {/* Header */}
   245	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground px-5 py-3 border-b-2 border-foreground sticky top-0 z-10">
   246	          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   247	            <RotateCcw size={22} />
   248	            <div>
   249	              <h2 className="text-xl font-extrabold uppercase tracking-tight">Process Return</h2>
   250	              <div className="font-mono font-bold text-[10px] opacity-90">
   251	                TXN: {lookedUpTx.id.slice(0, 8).toUpperCase()}…
   252	                {lookedUpTx.customerName && ` · ${lookedUpTx.customerName}`}
   253	              </div>
   254	            </div>
   255	          </div>
   256	          <button onClick={clearReturn} className="border-2 border-destructive-foreground p-1 hover:bg-foreground">
   257	            <X size={18} />
   258	          </button>
   259	        </div>
   260	
   261	        <div className="p-5">
   262	          {/* Original transaction info */}
   263	          <div className="border-2 border-foreground bg-background p-3 mb-4 flex items-center justify-between">
   264	            <div>
   265	              <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">Original Sale</div>
   266	              <div className="font-mono font-extrabold text-lg tabular-nums">{formatINR(lookedUpTx.total)}</div>
   267	            </div>
   268	            <div className="text-right">
   269	              <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">Method</div>
   270	              <div className="font-extrabold text-sm uppercase">{lookedUpTx.method}</div>
   271	            </div>
   272	            <div className="text-right">
   273	              <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">Date</div>
   274	              <div className="font-mono font-bold text-xs">{new Date(lookedUpTx.timestamp).toLocaleString("en-GB")}</div>
   275	            </div>
   276	          </div>
   277	
   278	          {/* Item list with checkboxes */}
   279	          <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">
   280	            Select Items to Return
   281	          </div>
   282	          <div className="border-2 border-foreground mb-4">
   283	            <div className="grid grid-cols-12 px-3 py-2 bg-foreground text-background text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">
   284	              <div className="col-span-1"></div>
   285	              <div className="col-span-5">Item</div>
   286	              <div className="col-span-2 text-center">Orig Qty</div>
   287	              <div className="col-span-2 text-center">Return Qty</div>
   288	              <div className="col-span-2 text-right">Refund</div>
   289	            </div>
   290	            {lookedUpTx.items.map((item, idx) => (
   291	              <div key={item.pid}
   292	                className={`grid grid-cols-12 px-3 py-2 items-center border-b border-foreground/30 last:border-b-0 cursor-pointer
   293	                  ${idx % 2 === 1 ? "bg-row-alt" : ""}
   294	                  ${item.selected ? "bg-destructive/10" : "opacity-60"}`}
   295	                onClick={() => toggleReturnItem(item.pid)}>
   296	                <div className="col-span-1">
   297	                  {item.selected
   298	                    ? <CheckSquare size={20} className="text-destructive" />
   299	                    : <Square size={20} className="text-muted-foreground" />}
   300	                </div>
   301	                <div className="col-span-5">
   302	                  <div className="font-extrabold text-sm leading-tight">{item.name}</div>
   303	                  <div className="font-mono text-[10px] font-bold text-muted-foreground">
   304	                    {item.pid} · {formatINR(item.unitPrice)}{item.weighed ? "/KG" : ""}
   305	                  </div>
   306	                </div>
   307	                <div className="col-span-2 text-center font-mono font-extrabold text-sm tabular-nums">
   308	                  {item.weighed ? item.originalQty.toFixed(2) : item.originalQty}
   309	                </div>
   310	                <div className="col-span-2 flex items-center justify-center gap-1" onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
   311	                  {item.selected ? (
   312	                    <>
   313	                      <button onClick={() => setReturnQty(item.pid, +(item.returnQty - (item.weighed ? 0.1 : 1)).toFixed(3))}
   314	                        className="border-2 border-foreground w-6 h-6 font-extrabold text-sm hover:bg-foreground hover:text-background">−</button>
   315	                      <span className="font-mono font-extrabold text-sm w-10 text-center tabular-nums">
   316	                        {item.weighed ? item.returnQty.toFixed(2) : item.returnQty}
   317	                      </span>
   318	                      <button onClick={() => setReturnQty(item.pid, +(item.returnQty + (item.weighed ? 0.1 : 1)).toFixed(3))}
   319	                        className="border-2 border-foreground w-6 h-6 font-extrabold text-sm hover:bg-foreground hover:text-background">+</button>
   320	                    </>
   321	                  ) : (
   322	                    <span className="font-mono text-sm text-muted-foreground">—</span>
   323	                  )}
   324	                </div>
   325	                <div className="col-span-2 text-right font-mono font-extrabold text-sm tabular-nums">
   326	                  {item.selected ? formatINR(item.unitPrice * item.returnQty) : "—"}
   327	                </div>
   328	              </div>
   329	            ))}
   330	          </div>
   331	
   332	          {/* Refund method */}
   333	          <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">Refund Payout Method</div>
   334	          <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mb-4">
   335	            {([
   336	              { m: "Cash" as PaymentMethod, icon: Banknote, label: "CASH" },
   337	              { m: "UPI" as PaymentMethod, icon: Smartphone, label: "UPI" },
   338	              { m: "Card" as PaymentMethod, icon: CreditCard, label: "CARD" },
   339	              { m: "Wallet" as PaymentMethod, icon: Wallet, label: "WALLET" },
   340	            ]).map(({ m, icon: Icon, label }) => (
   341	              <button key={m} onClick={() => setRefundMethod(m)}
   342	                className={`pressable border-2 border-foreground h-14 font-extrabold text-xs tracking-widest flex items-center justify-center gap-2
   343	                  ${refundMethod === m ? "bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground" : "bg-card hover:bg-secondary"}`}>
   344	                <Icon size={20} /> {label}
   345	              </button>
   346	            ))}
   347	          </div>
   348	          {lookedUpTx.method !== refundMethod && (
   349	            <div className="bg-warning text-warning-foreground border-2 border-foreground px-3 py-2 mb-4 flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">
   350	              <AlertTriangle size={14} />
   351	              Original payment was {lookedUpTx.method} · Refunding as {refundMethod}
   352	            </div>
   353	          )}
   354	
   355	          {returnError && (
   356	            <div className="bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground font-extrabold text-center py-2 mb-3 text-sm uppercase tracking-wider border-2 border-foreground">
   357	              {returnError}
   358	            </div>
   359	          )}
   360	
   361	          {/* Refund total */}
   362	          <div className="border-2 border-foreground mb-4">
   363	            <div className="flex items-end justify-between px-4 py-3 bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground">
   364	              <div>
   365	                <div className="text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-widest">Refund Total</div>
   366	                <div className="text-[10px] font-bold opacity-80">
   367	                  {selectedItems.length} item{selectedItems.length !== 1 && "s"} · {refundMethod}
   368	                </div>
   369	              </div>
   370	              <div className="font-mono font-extrabold tabular-nums leading-none" style={{ fontSize: 36 }}>
   371	                −{formatINR(refundTotal)}
   372	              </div>
   373	            </div>
   374	          </div>
   375	
   376	          {/* Action buttons */}
   377	          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
   378	            <button onClick={clearReturn}
   379	              className="pressable border-2 border-foreground bg-card h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest">
   380	              CANCEL
   381	            </button>
   382	            <button onClick={() => setShowPin(true)}
   383	              disabled={!canProcess || returnLoading}
   384	              className="pressable-primary bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground border-2 border-foreground h-14 font-extrabold tracking-widest text-base flex items-center justify-center gap-2 disabled:bg-muted disabled:text-muted-foreground disabled:shadow-none disabled:cursor-not-allowed">
   385	              <RotateCcw size={20} /> PROCESS REFUND
   386	            </button>
   387	          </div>
   388	        </div>
   389	      </div>
   390	
   391	      {/* Manager PIN auth overlay */}
   392	      {showPin && (
   393	        <ManagerPinModal
   394	          onSubmit={handleRefund}
   395	          onClose={() => setShowPin(false)}
   396	          loading={returnLoading}
   397	          error={returnError}
   398	        />
   399	      )}
   400	    </div>
   401	  );
   402	}

    46	def _set_auth_cookies(response, access_token, refresh_token):
    47	    """Reuse cookie-setting pattern from accounts."""
    48	    from django.conf import settings as s
    49	    kw = dict(
    50	        secure=s.JWT_AUTH_COOKIE_SECURE,
    51	        httponly=s.JWT_AUTH_COOKIE_HTTP_ONLY,
    52	        samesite=s.JWT_AUTH_COOKIE_SAMESITE,
    53	        path=s.JWT_AUTH_COOKIE_PATH,
    54	    )
    55	    response.set_cookie(key=s.JWT_AUTH_COOKIE, value=access_token, max_age=3600, **kw)
    56	    response.set_cookie(key=s.JWT_AUTH_REFRESH_COOKIE, value=refresh_token, max_age=86400, **kw)
    57	
    58	
    59	@method_decorator(csrf_exempt, name='dispatch')
    60	class PosLoginView(APIView):
    61	    """
    62	    POST /api/pos/login/
    63	    PIN-based login for POS terminals.
    64	    """
    65	    permission_classes = [AllowAny]
    66	
    67	    def post(self, request):
    68	        employee_id = request.data.get('employee_id', '')
    69	        pin = request.data.get('pin', '')
    70	
    71	        if not employee_id or not pin:
    72	            return Response(
    73	                {'error': 'employee_id and pin are required'},
    74	                status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
    75	            )
    76	
    77	        try:
    78	            employee = PosEmployee.objects.select_related('user').get(
    79	                employee_id=employee_id, pin=pin, is_active=True,
    80	            )
    81	        except PosEmployee.DoesNotExist:
    82	            return Response(
    83	                {'error': 'Invalid employee ID or PIN'},
    84	                status=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
    85	            )
    86	
    87	        user = employee.user
    88	        refresh = RefreshToken.for_user(user)
    89	        access_token = str(refresh.access_token)
    90	        refresh_token = str(refresh)
    91	
    92	        response = Response({
    93	            'message': 'POS login successful',
    94	            'access': access_token,
    95	            'refresh': refresh_token,
    96	            'employee_name': user.get_full_name() or user.username,
    97	        })
    98	        _set_auth_cookies(response, access_token, refresh_token)
    99	        return response
   100	
   101	
   102	@method_decorator(csrf_exempt, name='dispatch')
   103	class PosShiftOpenView(APIView):
   104	    """POST /api/pos/shift/open/"""
   105	    permission_classes = [IsPosOperator]
   106	
   107	    def post(self, request):
   108	        employee_id = request.data.get('employee_id', '')
   109	        opening_cash = request.data.get('opening_cash', 0)
   110	
   111	        try:
   112	            employee = PosEmployee.objects.get(
   113	                user=request.user, employee_id=employee_id,
   114	            )
   115	        except PosEmployee.DoesNotExist:
   116	            # Fallback: use user's employee record
   117	            try:
   118	                employee = request.user.pos_employee
   119	            except PosEmployee.DoesNotExist:
   120	                return Response(
   121	                    {'error': 'POS employee record not found'},
   122	                    status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
   123	                )
   124	
   125	        # Check for already-open shift
   126	        open_shift = PosShift.objects.filter(employee=employee, is_open=True).first()
   127	        if open_shift:
   128	            return Response({
   129	                'message': 'Shift already open',
   130	                'shift_id': str(open_shift.id),
   131	            })
   132	
   133	        shift = PosShift.objects.create(
   134	            employee=employee,
   135	            opening_cash=Decimal(str(opening_cash)),
   136	        )
   137	
   138	        return Response({
   139	            'message': 'Shift opened',
   140	            'shift_id': str(shift.id),
   141	        }, status=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)

   191	@method_decorator(csrf_exempt, name='dispatch')
   192	class PosProductsView(APIView):
   193	    """
   194	    GET /api/pos/products/
   195	    Derives POS catalog from inventory batches with stock > 0.
   196	    """
   197	    permission_classes = [IsPosOperator]
   198	
   199	    def get(self, request):
   200	        category = request.query_params.get('category')
   201	        search = request.query_params.get('search')
   202	
   203	        batches = InventoryBatch.objects.filter(
   204	            stock_level__gt=0,
   205	        ).select_related(
   206	            'variant', 'variant__product', 'variant__product__category',
   207	        )
   208	
   209	        if category:
   210	            batches = batches.filter(variant__product__category__slug=category)
   211	        if search:
   212	            batches = batches.filter(variant__product__name__icontains=search)
   213	
   214	        products = []
   215	        for batch in batches:
   216	            product = batch.variant.product
   217	            products.append({
   218	                'pid': str(batch.id),
   219	                'name': f"{product.name} ({batch.variant.unit})",
   220	                'price': float(batch.price),
   221	                'weighed': 'kg' in batch.variant.unit.lower() or 'g' in batch.variant.unit.lower(),
   222	                'category': product.category.name if product.category else '',
   223	                'stock': batch.stock_level,
   224	                'low_stock_threshold': 5,
   225	                'member_eligible': True,
   226	            })
   227	
   228	        serializer = PosProductSerializer(products, many=True)
   229	        return Response(serializer.data)
   230

   232	@method_decorator(csrf_exempt, name='dispatch')
   233	class PosCustomerLookupView(APIView):
   234	    """GET /api/pos/customers/lookup/?phone=..."""
   235	    permission_classes = [IsPosOperator]
   236	
   237	    def get(self, request):
   238	        phone = request.query_params.get('phone', '')
   239	        if not phone:
   240	            return Response({'error': 'phone parameter required'}, status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)
   241	
   242	        try:
   243	            customer = PosCustomer.objects.get(phone=phone)
   244	            return Response(PosCustomerSerializer(customer).data)
   245	        except PosCustomer.DoesNotExist:
   246	            return Response({'error': 'Customer not found'}, status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND)

   249	@method_decorator(csrf_exempt, name='dispatch')
   250	class PosCustomerCreateView(APIView):
   251	    """POST /api/pos/customers/"""
   252	    permission_classes = [IsPosOperator]
   253	
   254	    def post(self, request):
   255	        name = request.data.get('name', '')
   256	        phone = request.data.get('phone', '')
   257	        email = request.data.get('email', '')
   258	
   259	        if not name or not phone:
   260	            return Response({'error': 'name and phone required'}, status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)
   261	
   262	        customer, created = PosCustomer.objects.get_or_create(
   263	            phone=phone,
   264	            defaults={'name': name, 'email': email},
   265	        )
   266	
   267	        if not created:
   268	            return Response(
   269	                {'error': 'Customer with this phone already exists'},
   270	                status=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT,
   271	            )
   272	
   273	        return Response(PosCustomerSerializer(customer).data, status=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)

   276	@method_decorator(csrf_exempt, name='dispatch')
   277	class PosOrderCreateView(APIView):
   278	    """POST /api/pos/orders/"""
   279	    permission_classes = [IsPosOperator]
   280	
   281	    def post(self, request):
   282	        serializer = PosOrderCreateSerializer(data=request.data)
   283	        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)
   284	        data = serializer.validated_data
   285	
   286	        try:
   287	            employee = request.user.pos_employee
   288	        except PosEmployee.DoesNotExist:
   289	            return Response({'error': 'Employee not found'}, status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND)
   290	
   291	        shift = PosShift.objects.filter(employee=employee, is_open=True).first()
   292	        if not shift:
   293	            return Response({'error': 'No open shift'}, status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)
   294	
   295	        # Resolve customer
   296	        customer = None
   297	        customer_id = data.get('customer_id')
   298	        if customer_id:
   299	            try:
   300	                customer = PosCustomer.objects.get(id=customer_id)
   301	            except (PosCustomer.DoesNotExist, Exception):
   302	                pass
   303	
   304	        # Determine payment method
   305	        tenders = data.get('tenders', [])
   306	        method = tenders[0]['method'] if len(tenders) == 1 else 'Split'
   307	
   308	        with transaction.atomic():
   309	            txn = PosTransaction.objects.create(
   310	                shift=shift,
   311	                customer=customer,
   312	                method=method,
   313	                subtotal=data['subtotal'],
   314	                member_discount=data.get('member_discount', 0),
   315	                surcharge=data.get('surcharge', 0),
   316	                total=data['total'],
   317	                receipt_delivery=data.get('receipt_delivery', ''),
   318	            )
   319	
   320	            # Create items
   321	            for item in data['items']:
   322	                PosTransactionItem.objects.create(
   323	                    transaction=txn,
   324	                    pid=item['pid'],
   325	                    name=item['name'],
   326	                    unit_price=Decimal(str(item['unit_price'])),
   327	                    weighed=item.get('weighed', False),
   328	                    quantity=Decimal(str(item['quantity'])),
   329	                    member_eligible=item.get('member_eligible', False),
   330	                )
   331	
   332	                # Deduct Stock from InventoryBatch
   333	                try:
   334	                    InventoryBatch.objects.filter(id=item['pid']).update(
   335	                        stock_level=F('stock_level') - Decimal(str(item['quantity']))
   336	                    )
   337	                except Exception:
   338	                    # Log error but don't fail transaction? 
   339	                    # Usually better to fail if stock is critical, 
   340	                    # but here we allow it for now.
   341	                    pass
   342	
   343	            # Create tenders
   344	            for tender in tenders:
   345	                PosTender.objects.create(
   346	                    transaction=txn,
   347	                    method=tender['method'],
   348	                    amount=Decimal(str(tender['amount'])),
   349	                )
   350	
   351	            # Update shift totals
   352	            shift.txn_count += 1
   353	            shift.total_sales += txn.total
   354	            if method == 'Cash' or any(t['method'] == 'Cash' for t in tenders):
   355	                cash_amount = sum(
   356	                    Decimal(str(t['amount'])) for t in tenders if t['method'] == 'Cash'
   357	                )
   358	                shift.cash_sales += cash_amount
   359	            shift.save()
   360	
   361	        return Response(PosTransactionSerializer(txn).data, status=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
   362	
   363	
   364	@method_decorator(csrf_exempt, name='dispatch')
   365	class PosWastageView(APIView):
   366	    """
   367	    POST /api/pos/wastage/ — Log wastage
   368	    GET  /api/pos/wastage/ — Get wastage for current shift
   369	    """
   370	    permission_classes = [IsPosOperator]
   371	
   372	    def get(self, request):
   373	        try:
   374	            employee = request.user.pos_employee
   375	        except PosEmployee.DoesNotExist:
   376	            return Response([], status=status.HTTP_200_OK)
   377	
   378	        shift = PosShift.objects.filter(employee=employee).order_by('-started_at').first()
   379	        if not shift:
   380	            return Response([], status=status.HTTP_200_OK)
   381	
   382	        logs = shift.wastage_logs.all()
   383	        serializer = PosWastageSerializer(logs, many=True)
   384	        return Response(serializer.data)
   385	
   386	    def post(self, request):
   387	        try:
   388	            employee = request.user.pos_employee
   389	        except PosEmployee.DoesNotExist:
   390	            return Response({'error': 'Employee not found'}, status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND)
   391	
   392	        shift = PosShift.objects.filter(employee=employee, is_open=True).first()
   393	        if not shift:
   394	            return Response({'error': 'No open shift'}, status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)
   395	
   396	        pid = request.data.get('pid', '')
   397	        name = request.data.get('name', '')
   398	        quantity = request.data.get('quantity', 0)
   399	        weighed = request.data.get('weighed', False)
   400	        unit_price = request.data.get('unit_price', 0)
   401	        reason = request.data.get('reason', 'Spoiled')
   402	
   403	        log = PosWastageLog.objects.create(
   404	            shift=shift,
   405	            pid=pid,
   406	            name=name,
   407	            quantity=Decimal(str(quantity)),
   408	            weighed=weighed,
   409	            unit_price=Decimal(str(unit_price)),
   410	            reason=reason,
   411	        )
   412	
   413	        # Deduct Stock for wastage
   414	        try:
   415	            InventoryBatch.objects.filter(id=pid).update(
   416	                stock_level=F('stock_level') - Decimal(str(quantity))
   417	            )
   418	        except Exception:
   419	            pass
   420	
   421	        return Response({
   422	            'message': 'Wastage logged',
   423	            'id': str(log.id),
   424	        }, status=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
   425

   427	@method_decorator(csrf_exempt, name='dispatch')
   428	class PosOrderLookupView(APIView):
   429	    """
   430	    GET /api/pos/orders/lookup/?receipt_id=...
   431	    Look up a past transaction by its UUID for return processing.
   432	    """
   433	    permission_classes = [IsPosOperator]
   434	
   435	    def get(self, request):
   436	        receipt_id = request.query_params.get('receipt_id', '').strip()
   437	        if not receipt_id:
   438	            return Response(
   439	                {'error': 'receipt_id parameter required'},
   440	                status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
   441	            )
   442	
   443	        try:
   444	            # Try full UUID first, then fallback to prefix match
   445	            if len(receipt_id) >= 8:
   446	                txn = PosTransaction.objects.prefetch_related('items', 'tenders').filter(id__istartswith=receipt_id).first()
   447	            else:
   448	                txn = PosTransaction.objects.prefetch_related('items', 'tenders').get(id=receipt_id)
   449	            
   450	            if not txn:
   451	                raise PosTransaction.DoesNotExist()
   452	        except (PosTransaction.DoesNotExist, Exception):
   453	            return Response(
   454	                {'error': 'Transaction not found'},
   455	                status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
   456	            )
   457	
   458	        # Don't allow looking up RETURN transactions for another return
   459	        if txn.transaction_type == 'RETURN':
   460	            return Response(
   461	                {'error': 'Cannot return a return transaction'},
   462	                status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
   463	            )
   464	
   465	        serializer = PosTransactionSerializer(txn)
   466	        data = serializer.data
   467	        data['transaction_type'] = txn.transaction_type
   468	        return Response(data)
   469	
   470	
   471	@method_decorator(csrf_exempt, name='dispatch')
   472	class PosRefundView(APIView):
   473	    """
   474	    POST /api/pos/orders/refund/
   475	    Process a return/refund for a previous transaction.
   476	
   477	    Payload:
   478	      {
   479	        "original_transaction_id": "uuid",
   480	        "manager_pin": "1234",
   481	        "items": [{"pid": "...", "quantity": 1.0}],  // items being returned
   482	        "refund_method": "Cash"  // how the refund is paid out
   483	      }
   484	
   485	    Business rules:
   486	      - Manager PIN must match an employee with is_manager=True
   487	      - Creates a RETURN PosTransaction with negative totals
   488	      - Restocks returned items in InventoryBatch
   489	      - Deducts from shift totals
   490	    """
   491	    permission_classes = [IsPosOperator]
   492	
   493	    def post(self, request):
   494	        original_id = request.data.get('original_transaction_id', '')
   495	        manager_pin = request.data.get('manager_pin', '')
   496	        return_items = request.data.get('items', [])
   497	        refund_method = request.data.get('refund_method', 'Cash')
   498	
   499	        # ── Validate inputs ──
   500	        if not original_id or not manager_pin or not return_items:
   501	            return Response(
   502	                {'error': 'original_transaction_id, manager_pin, and items are required'},
   503	                status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
   504	            )
   505	
   506	        # ── Verify manager PIN ──
   507	        try:
   508	            manager = PosEmployee.objects.get(
   509	                pin=manager_pin, is_manager=True, is_active=True,
   510	            )
   511	        except PosEmployee.DoesNotExist:
   512	            return Response(
   513	                {'error': 'Invalid manager PIN'},
   514	                status=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,
   515	            )
   516	
   517	        # ── Fetch original transaction ──
   518	        try:
   519	            original_txn = PosTransaction.objects.prefetch_related(
   520	                'items', 'tenders'
   521	            ).get(id=original_id, transaction_type='SALE')
   522	        except (PosTransaction.DoesNotExist, Exception):
   523	            return Response(
   524	                {'error': 'Original sale transaction not found'},
   525	                status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
   526	            )
   527	
   528	        # ── Get current employee & shift ──
   529	        try:
   530	            employee = request.user.pos_employee
   531	        except PosEmployee.DoesNotExist:
   532	            return Response(
   533	                {'error': 'Employee not found'},
   534	                status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
   535	            )
   536	
   537	        shift = PosShift.objects.filter(employee=employee, is_open=True).first()
   538	        if not shift:
   539	            return Response(
   540	                {'error': 'No open shift'},
   541	                status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
   542	            )
   543	
   544	        # ── Build return items & calculate refund total ──
   545	        original_items = {item.pid: item for item in original_txn.items.all()}
   546	        refund_subtotal = Decimal('0')
   547	        validated_items = []
   548	
   549	        for ri in return_items:
   550	            pid = ri.get('pid', '')
   551	            qty = Decimal(str(ri.get('quantity', 0)))
   552	
   553	            if pid not in original_items:
   554	                return Response(
   555	                    {'error': f'Item {pid} not found in original transaction'},
   556	                    status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
   557	                )
   558	
   559	            orig_item = original_items[pid]
   560	            if qty > orig_item.quantity:
   561	                return Response(
   562	                    {'error': f'Return quantity for {pid} exceeds original quantity'},
   563	                    status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
   564	                )
   565	
   566	            item_total = orig_item.unit_price * qty
   567	            refund_subtotal += item_total
   568	            validated_items.append({
   569	                'pid': pid,
   570	                'name': orig_item.name,
   571	                'unit_price': orig_item.unit_price,
   572	                'weighed': orig_item.weighed,
   573	                'quantity': qty,
   574	                'member_eligible': orig_item.member_eligible,
   575	            })
   576	
   577	        refund_total = refund_subtotal  # Could apply surcharge reversal if needed
   578	
   579	        with transaction.atomic():
   580	            # ── Create RETURN transaction (negative totals) ──
   581	            return_txn = PosTransaction.objects.create(
   582	                shift=shift,
   583	                customer=original_txn.customer,
   584	                transaction_type='RETURN',
   585	                related_transaction=original_txn,
   586	                method=refund_method,
   587	                subtotal=-refund_subtotal,
   588	                member_discount=Decimal('0'),
   589	                surcharge=Decimal('0'),
   590	                total=-refund_total,
   591	            )
   592	
   593	            # ── Create return line items ──
   594	            for item in validated_items:
   595	                PosTransactionItem.objects.create(
   596	                    transaction=return_txn,
   597	                    pid=item['pid'],
   598	                    name=item['name'],
   599	                    unit_price=item['unit_price'],
   600	                    weighed=item['weighed'],
   601	                    quantity=item['quantity'],
   602	                    member_eligible=item['member_eligible'],
   603	                )
   604	
   605	            # ── Create refund tender ──
   606	            PosTender.objects.create(
   607	                transaction=return_txn,
   608	                method=refund_method,
   609	                amount=-refund_total,
   610	            )
   611	
   612	            # ── Restock inventory ──
   613	            for item in validated_items:
   614	                try:
   615	                    InventoryBatch.objects.filter(id=item['pid']).update(
   616	                        stock_level=F('stock_level') + item['quantity']
   617	                    )
   618	                except Exception:
   619	                    pass  # PID may not map directly to a batch ID
   620	
   621	            # ── Deduct from shift totals ──
   622	            shift.txn_count += 1
   623	            shift.total_sales -= refund_total
   624	            if refund_method == 'Cash':
   625	                shift.cash_sales -= refund_total
   626	            shift.save()
   627	
   628	        result = PosTransactionSerializer(return_txn).data
   629	        result['transaction_type'] = 'RETURN'
   630	        result['original_transaction_id'] = str(original_id)
   631	        result['authorized_by'] = manager.employee_id
   632	
   633	        return Response(result, status=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)

# Tauri Plugin Printer
Interface with printers through [Powershell](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/powershell/scripting/install/installing-powershell-on-windows?view=powershell-7.3)


## Buy Me Coffee
[PayPal](https://paypal.me/alfianlensun)

[BuyMeCoffee](https://www.buymeacoffee.com/alfianlensun)


## Install
> If you are installing from npm and crate.io package registry, make sure the mayor and minor versions for both packages are the same, otherwise, the API may not match.

Crate: https://crates.io/crates/tauri-plugin-printer

Install latest version:

`cargo add tauri-plugin-printer`

Or add the following to your `Cargo.toml` for spesific version:

`src-tauri/Cargo.toml`

```toml
[dependencies]
tauri-plugin-printer = { version = "1.0.10" }
```

You can install the JavaScript Guest bindings using your preferred JavaScript package manager:

```sh
pnpm add tauri-plugin-printer
# or
npm add tauri-plugin-printer
# or
yarn add tauri-plugin-printer
```

## Usage

First you need to register the core plugin with Tauri:

`src-tauri/src/main.rs`

```rust
fn main() {
    tauri::Builder::default()
        .plugin(tauri_plugin_printer::init())  
        .run(tauri::generate_context!())
        .expect("error while running tauri application");
}
```

Afterwards all the plugin's APIs are available through the JavaScript guest bindings:

```javascript
import {printers, print, print_file, jobs, job, restart_job, pause_job, resume_job, remove_job} from "tauri-plugin-printer";

// get list printers
const list = await printers()

// get printer by id
const list = await printers(id)


const data = [
    {
        type: 'image',
        url: 'https://randomuser.me/api/portraits/men/43.jpg',     // file path

// export const print = async (data: PrintData, options: PrintOptions) => {
const print = async (data, options) => {
    const html = document.createElement('html');
    const container = document.createElement("div");
    container.id = "wrapper";
    container.style.position = "relative";
    container.style.display = "flex";
    container.style.backgroundColor = "#fff";
    container.style.flexDirection = "column";
    container.style.alignItems = "center";
    container.style.justifyContent = "flex-start";
    container.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    container.style.width = `300px`;
    container.style.height = "fit-content";
    container.style.color = "#000";
    container.style.fontSize = '12px';
    for (const item of data) {
        if (item.type == 'image') {
            const wrapperImage = document.createElement('div');
            wrapperImage.style.width = "100%";
            if (item?.position == "center") {
                wrapperImage.style.display = 'flex';
                wrapperImage.style.justifyContent = 'center';
            }
            if (typeof item.url == "undefined")
                throw new Error('Image required {url}');
            const image = document.createElement('img');
            image.width = 100,
                image.height = 100;
            const client = await (0, http_1.getClient)();
            const response = await client.get(item.url, {
                responseType: http_1.ResponseType.Binary
            });
            image.src = `data:${mime_1.default.getType(item.url)};base64,${buffer_1.Buffer.from(response.data).toString('base64')}`;
            if (item.width) {
                image.width = item.width;
            }
            if (item.height) {
                image.height = item.height;
            }
            if (item.style) {
                const styles = item.style;
                for (const style of Object.keys(styles)) {
                    const key = style;
                    image.style[key] = styles[key];
                }
            }
            wrapperImage.appendChild(image);
            container.appendChild(wrapperImage);
        }
        if (item.type == 'text') {
            const textWrapper = document.createElement('div');
            textWrapper.style.width = "100%";
            if (item.value) {
                textWrapper.innerHTML = item.value;
            }
            if (item.style) {
                const styles = item.style;
                for (const style of Object.keys(styles)) {
                    const key = style;
                    textWrapper.style[key] = styles[key];
                }

/**
 * Print File.
 * @params first_param: File Path, second_param: Print Setting
 * @returns A process status.
 */
const print_file = async (options) => {
    if (options.id == undefined && options.name == undefined)
        throw new Error('print_file require id | name as string');
    if (options.path == undefined && options.file == undefined)
        throw new Error('print_file require parameter path as string | file as Buffer');
    let id = "";
    if (typeof options.id != 'undefined') {
        id = decodeBase64(options.id);
    }
    else {
        id = options.name;
    }
    const printerSettings = {
        paper: 'A4',
        method: 'simplex',
        scale: 'noscale',
        orientation: 'portrait',
        repeat: 1
    };
    if (typeof options?.print_setting?.paper != "undefined")
        printerSettings.paper = options.print_setting.paper;
    if (typeof options?.print_setting?.method != "undefined")
        printerSettings.method = options.print_setting.method;
    if (typeof options?.print_setting?.scale != "undefined")
        printerSettings.scale = options.print_setting.scale;
    if (typeof options?.print_setting?.orientation != "undefined")
        printerSettings.orientation = options.print_setting.orientation;
    if (typeof options?.print_setting?.repeat != "undefined")
        printerSettings.repeat = options.print_setting.repeat;
    if (typeof options?.print_setting?.range != "undefined")
        printerSettings.range = options.print_setting.range;
    if (typeof options.path != "undefined") {
        if (options.path.split('.').length <= 1)
            throw new Error('File not supported');
        if (options.path.split('.').pop() != 'pdf')
            throw new Error('File not supported');
    }
    let rangeStr = "";
    if (printerSettings.range) {
        if (typeof printerSettings.range == 'string') {
            if (!(new RegExp(/^[0-9,]+$/).test(printerSettings.range)))
                throw new Error('Invalid range value ');
            rangeStr = printerSettings.range[printerSettings.range.length - 1] != "," ? printerSettings.range : printerSettings.range.substring(0, printerSettings.range.length - 1);
        }
        else if (printerSettings.range.from) {
            rangeStr = `${printerSettings.range.from}-${printerSettings.range.to}`;
        }
    }

fn open_cash_drawer() -> Result<(), String> {
    #[cfg(windows)]

<div align="center">

# Tauri Plugin Printer V2

[![Crates.io](https://img.shields.io/crates/v/tauri-plugin-printer-v2.svg)](https://crates.io/crates/tauri-plugin-printer-v2)
[![NPM](https://img.shields.io/npm/v/tauri-plugin-printer-api.svg)](https://www.npmjs.com/package/tauri-plugin-printer-api)
[![License](https://img.shields.io/badge/license-MIT-blue.svg)](LICENSE)
[![Tauri](https://img.shields.io/badge/Tauri-v2.0-orange.svg)](https://tauri.app/)

**一个功能强大的 Tauri V2 打印机插件**

支持 PDF/HTML 打印、打印机管理、任务控制等完整功能

[安装](#-安装) • [使用](#-使用方法) • [API文档](#-api-文档) • [示例](#-示例)

</div>

---

## 🚀 快速开始

### 5分钟上手指南

1. **安装插件**
   ```bash
   cargo add tauri-plugin-printer-v2
   npm i tauri-plugin-printer-v2
   ```

2. **注册插件**
   ```rust
   // src-tauri/src/lib.rs
   use tauri_plugin_printer_v2::init;
   
   #[cfg_attr(mobile, tauri::mobile_entry_point)]
   pub fn run() {
       tauri::Builder::default()
           .plugin(init())
           .run(tauri::generate_context!())
           .expect("error while running tauri application");
   }
   ```

3. **配置权限**
   ```json
   // src-tauri/capabilities/default.json
   {
     "permissions": [
       "printer:allow-get-printers",
       "printer:allow-print-pdf",
       "printer:allow-print-html"
     ]
   }
   ```

4. **开始使用**
   ```javascript
   import { getPrinters, printPdf } from 'tauri-plugin-printer-v2';
   
   // 获取打印机
   const printers = JSON.parse(await getPrinters());
   console.log('可用打印机:', printers);
   
   // 打印PDF
   await printPdf({
     path: '/path/to/document.pdf',
     printer: printers[0].name
   });
   ```

🎉 **恭喜！** 您已成功集成打印机插件，现在可以开始打印文档了。

## 致谢

本项目基于以下开源项目开发：
- [alfianlensundev/tauri-plugin-printer](https://github.com/alfianlensundev/tauri-plugin-printer) - 原始 Tauri 打印机插件
- [adao99/tauri-plugin-printer-v2](https://github.com/adao99/tauri-plugin-printer-v2) - Tauri v2.0 版本的打印机插件

感谢原作者们的贡献和开源精神。

## ✨ 特性

- 🖨️ 获取系统打印机列表
- 📄 打印 PDF 文件
- 🌐 打印 HTML 内容
- 📋 管理打印任务（暂停、恢复、重启、删除）
- 🔍 按名称查询打印机
- 📊 获取打印任务状态
- 🌐 支持中文打印机名称
- 🔧 完全兼容 Tauri V2 稳定版

## 📦 安装

### 方法一：使用 crates.io（推荐）

```bash
# 添加 Rust 依赖
cargo add tauri-plugin-printer-v2

# 安装前端 API
npm i tauri-plugin-printer-v2
```

### 方法二：使用 Tauri CLI

```bash
npx tauri add https://github.com/chen-collab/tauri-plugin-printer
```

### 方法三：手动安装

1. 在 `Cargo.toml` 中添加依赖：

```toml
[dependencies]
tauri-plugin-printer-v2 = "0.2.0"
# 或使用 Git 版本
# tauri-plugin-printer-v2 = { git = "https://github.com/chen-collab/tauri-plugin-printer", branch = "chen" }
```

2. 在 `src-tauri/src/lib.rs` 中注册插件：

```rust
use tauri_plugin_printer_v2::init;

#[cfg_attr(mobile, tauri::mobile_entry_point)]
pub fn run() {
    tauri::Builder::default()
        .plugin(init())
        .run(tauri::generate_context!())
        .expect("error while running tauri application");
}
```

3. 在 `src-tauri/capabilities/default.json` 中添加权限：

```json
{
  "permissions": [
    "printer:default"
  ]
}
```

4. 安装前端依赖：

```bash
npm i tauri-plugin-printer-v2
```

## 🚀 使用方法

### 基础示例

```javascript
import { ping, getPrinters } from 'tauri-plugin-printer-v2';

// 测试插件连接
const response = await ping({ value: 'Hello from frontend!' });
console.log(response);

// 获取打印机列表
const printers = await getPrinters();
console.log('可用打印机:', printers);
```

### 完整 API 示例

```javascript
import {
  ping,
  getPrinters,
  getPrintersByName,
  printPdf,
  printHtml,
  getJobs,
  getJobsById,
  resumeJob,
  restartJob,
  pauseJob,
  removeJob
} from 'tauri-plugin-printer-v2';

// 1. 获取所有打印机
const allPrinters = await getPrinters();

// 2. 按名称获取特定打印机
const specificPrinter = await getPrintersByName('Microsoft Print to PDF');

// 3. 打印 PDF 文件
const printResult = await printPdf({
  path: '/path/to/your/file.pdf',
  printer: 'Microsoft Print to PDF',
  pages: '1-3',
  subset: 'odd'
});

// 4. 打印 HTML 内容
const htmlPrintResult = await printHtml({
  html: '<h1>Hello World</h1><p>这是一个HTML打印测试</p>',
  printer: 'Microsoft Print to PDF'
});

// 4.1 使用自定义纸张大小打印 HTML
const customSizeHtmlResult = await printHtml({
  html: '<h1>自定义尺寸</h1><p>使用 200mm x 300mm 的自定义纸张</p>',
  printer: 'Microsoft Print to PDF',
  page_width: 200,  // 宽度 200mm
  page_height: 300, // 高度 300mm
  orientation: 'portrait'
});

// 5. 获取打印任务
const jobs = await getJobs('Microsoft Print to PDF');

// 6. 管理打印任务
const jobId = '123';
const printerName = 'Microsoft Print to PDF';

// 暂停任务
await pauseJob(printerName, jobId);

// 恢复任务
await resumeJob(printerName, jobId);

// 重启任务
await restartJob(printerName, jobId);

// 删除任务
await removeJob(printerName, jobId);
```

## 📋 示例

### 实际应用场景

#### 1. 打印发票或报告

```javascript
import { printHtml, getPrinters } from 'tauri-plugin-printer-v2';

// 生成发票HTML
const invoiceHtml = `
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8">
    <title>发票</title>
    <style>
        body { font-family: Arial, sans-serif; margin: 20px; }
        .header { text-align: center; margin-bottom: 30px; }
        .invoice-details { margin-bottom: 20px; }
        table { width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; }
        th, td { border: 1px solid #ddd; padding: 8px; text-align: left; }
        th { background-color: #f2f2f2; }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="header">
        <h1>发票</h1>
        <p>发票号码: INV-2024-001</p>
    </div>
    <div class="invoice-details">
        <p><strong>客户:</strong> 张三</p>
        <p><strong>日期:</strong> 2024-01-15</p>
    </div>
    <table>
        <tr><th>项目</th><th>数量</th><th>单价</th><th>总计</th></tr>
        <tr><td>产品A</td><td>2</td><td>¥100</td><td>¥200</td></tr>
        <tr><td>产品B</td><td>1</td><td>¥150</td><td>¥150</td></tr>
    </table>
    <p style="text-align: right; margin-top: 20px;"><strong>总计: ¥350</strong></p>
</body>
</html>
`;

// 打印发票
try {
    const result = await printHtml({
        html: invoiceHtml,
        printer: 'Microsoft Print to PDF' // 或选择其他打印机
    });
    console.log('发票打印成功:', result);
} catch (error) {
    console.error('打印失败:', error);
}
```

#### 2. 批量打印PDF文件

```javascript
import { printPdf, getPrinters } from 'tauri-plugin-printer-v2';

const pdfFiles = [
    '/path/to/document1.pdf',
    '/path/to/document2.pdf',
    '/path/to/document3.pdf'
];

// 获取默认打印机
const printers = JSON.parse(await getPrinters());
const defaultPrinter = printers.find(p => p.is_default)?.name || printers[0]?.name;

// 批量打印
for (const filePath of pdfFiles) {
    try {
        await printPdf({
            path: filePath,
            printer: defaultPrinter,
            pages: '1-10' // 只打印前10页
        });
        console.log(`已打印: ${filePath}`);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error(`打印失败 ${filePath}:`, error);
    }
}
```

#### 3. 打印机状态监控

```javascript
import { getPrinters, getJobs } from 'tauri-plugin-printer-v2';

// 监控打印机状态
async function monitorPrinters() {
    try {
        const printers = JSON.parse(await getPrinters());
        
        for (const printer of printers) {
            console.log(`打印机: ${printer.name}`);
            console.log(`状态: ${printer.status}`);
            console.log(`是否默认: ${printer.is_default ? '是' : '否'}`);
            
            // 获取打印任务
            const jobs = JSON.parse(await getJobs(printer.name));
            console.log(`待处理任务: ${jobs.length}`);
            
            console.log('---');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('获取打印机信息失败:', error);
    }
}

// 每30秒检查一次
setInterval(monitorPrinters, 30000);
```

## 📚 API 文档

### `ping(request: PingRequest): Promise<PingResponse>`
测试插件连接状态。

### `getPrinters(): Promise<string>`
获取系统中所有可用的打印机列表，返回 JSON 格式的字符串。

### `getPrintersByName(name: string): Promise<string>`
根据打印机名称获取特定打印机信息。

### `printPdf(options: PrintOptions): Promise<string>`
打印 PDF 文件。

**PrintOptions 参数：**
- `path`: PDF 文件路径
- `printer`: 打印机名称
- `pages`: 页面范围（可选）
- `subset`: 页面子集（可选）

### `printHtml(options: HtmlPrintOptions): Promise<string>`
打印 HTML 内容，支持自定义纸张大小。

**HtmlPrintOptions 参数：**
- `html`: HTML 内容字符串
- `printer`: 打印机名称
- `page_width`: 自定义页面宽度（毫米，可选）
- `page_height`: 自定义页面高度（毫米，可选）
- `page_size`: 预定义纸张大小（如 A4、A3、Letter 等，可选）
- `orientation`: 页面方向（portrait/landscape，可选）
- `margin`: 页边距设置（可选）
- `quality`: 打印质量（可选）
- `grayscale`: 是否灰度打印（可选）
- `copies`: 打印份数（可选）

### 打印任务管理

- `getJobs(printer: string): Promise<string>` - 获取打印机的所有任务
- `getJobsById(printer: string, jobId: string): Promise<string>` - 获取特定任务信息
- `pauseJob(printer: string, jobId: string): Promise<string>` - 暂停打印任务
- `resumeJob(printer: string, jobId: string): Promise<string>` - 恢复打印任务
- `restartJob(printer: string, jobId: string): Promise<string>` - 重启打印任务
- `removeJob(printer: string, jobId: string): Promise<string>` - 删除打印任务

## 🛠️ 开发

### 运行示例应用

```bash
# 克隆仓库
git clone https://github.com/chen-collab/tauri-plugin-printer.git
cd tauri-plugin-printer

# 构建插件
npm run build

# 运行示例应用
cd examples/tauri-app
npm install
npm run tauri:dev
```

### 项目结构

```
tauri-plugin-printer/
├── src/                    # Rust 源代码
│   ├── lib.rs             # 插件主入口
│   ├── commands.rs        # Tauri 命令定义
│   ├── desktop.rs         # 桌面端实现
│   ├── windows.rs         # Windows 特定实现
│   └── ...
├── guest-js/              # JavaScript API
│   └── index.ts           # 前端 API 定义
├── permissions/           # 权限配置
├── examples/              # 示例应用
│   └── tauri-app/         # Vue.js 示例
└── dist-js/               # 构建后的 JS 文件
```

## 🔧 权限配置

插件使用以下权限：

```toml
[default]
description = "Default permissions for the plugin"
permissions = [
  "allow-ping",
  "allow-create-temp-file", 
  "allow-remove-temp-file", 
  "allow-get-printers", 
  "allow-get-printers-by-name", 
  "allow-print-pdf", 
  "allow-print-html",
  "allow-get-jobs", 
  "allow-get-jobs-by-id", 
  "allow-resume-job", 
  "allow-restart-job", 
  "allow-pause-job", 
  "allow-remove-job"
]
```

## 🐛 已知问题

- 目前主要支持 Windows 系统
- 某些打印机驱动可能不完全兼容
- 大文件打印可能需要额外的内存管理
- HTML 打印在某些复杂布局下可能出现格式问题

## 🔧 故障排除

### 常见问题

#### Q: 无法获取打印机列表
**A:** 请检查以下几点：
- 确保系统中已安装打印机
- 检查打印机服务是否正常运行
- 确认应用具有访问打印机的权限

#### Q: PDF 打印失败
**A:** 可能的解决方案：
- 确保 PDF 文件路径正确且文件存在
- 检查 PDF 文件是否损坏
- 确认系统已安装 PDF 阅读器（如 Adobe Reader）
- 尝试使用绝对路径而非相对路径

#### Q: HTML 打印格式不正确
**A:** 建议：
- 使用简单的 CSS 样式，避免复杂的布局
- 设置合适的页面大小和边距
- 测试时先打印到 PDF 查看效果
- 避免使用 JavaScript 和外部资源

#### Q: 权限配置问题
**A:** 确保在 `src-tauri/capabilities/default.json` 中正确配置了权限：
```json
{
  "permissions": [
    "printer:allow-ping",
    "printer:allow-get-printers",
    "printer:allow-get-printers-by-name",
    "printer:allow-print-pdf",
    "printer:allow-print-html",
    "printer:allow-get-jobs",
    "printer:allow-restart-job",
    "printer:allow-pause-job",
    "printer:allow-resume-job",
    "printer:allow-remove-job"
  ]
}
```

### 调试技巧

1. **启用详细日志**：
   ```bash
   RUST_LOG=debug npm run tauri dev
   ```

2. **检查打印机状态**：
   ```javascript
   const printers = JSON.parse(await getPrinters());
   console.log('可用打印机:', printers);
   ```

3. **测试连接**：
   ```javascript
   try {
     const result = await ping();
     console.log('插件连接正常:', result);
   } catch (error) {
     console.error('插件连接失败:', error);
   }
   ```

## ⚡ 性能优化

### 最佳实践

#### 1. 打印大文件时的优化

```javascript
// 对于大型PDF文件，建议分页打印
const largePdfPath = '/path/to/large-document.pdf';

// 分批打印，每次10页
for (let startPage = 1; startPage <= totalPages; startPage += 10) {
    const endPage = Math.min(startPage + 9, totalPages);
    
    await printPdf({
        path: largePdfPath,
        printer: printerName,
        pages: `${startPage}-${endPage}`
    });
    
    // 添加延迟避免打印队列过载
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
}
```

#### 2. HTML 打印优化

```javascript
// 优化的HTML结构
const optimizedHtml = `
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8">
    <style>
        /* 打印专用样式 */
        @media print {
            body { margin: 0; padding: 20px; }
            .no-print { display: none; }
            .page-break { page-break-before: always; }
        }
        
        /* 基础样式 */
        body {
            font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif;
            font-size: 12pt;
            line-height: 1.4;
        }
        
        table {
            width: 100%;
            border-collapse: collapse;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
        }
        
        th, td {
            border: 1px solid #000;
            padding: 8px;
            text-align: left;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <!-- 内容 -->
</body>
</html>
`;
```

#### 3. 错误处理和重试机制

```javascript
// 带重试的打印函数
async function printWithRetry(printFunction, options, maxRetries = 3) {
    for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++) {
        try {
            const result = await printFunction(options);
            return result;
        } catch (error) {
            console.warn(`打印尝试 ${attempt} 失败:`, error.message);
            
            if (attempt === maxRetries) {
                throw new Error(`打印失败，已重试 ${maxRetries} 次: ${error.message}`);
            }
            
            // 指数退避延迟
            const delay = Math.pow(2, attempt) * 1000;
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
        }
    }
}

// 使用示例
try {
    await printWithRetry(printPdf, {
        path: '/path/to/document.pdf',
        printer: 'HP LaserJet'
    });
} catch (error) {
    console.error('最终打印失败:', error);
}
```

#### 4. 打印队列管理

```javascript
class PrintQueue {
    constructor(maxConcurrent = 2) {
        this.queue = [];
        this.running = [];
        this.maxConcurrent = maxConcurrent;
    }
    
    async add(printTask) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            this.queue.push({ task: printTask, resolve, reject });
            this.process();
        });
    }
    
    async process() {
        if (this.running.length >= this.maxConcurrent || this.queue.length === 0) {
            return;
        }
        
        const { task, resolve, reject } = this.queue.shift();
        const promise = task().then(resolve).catch(reject);
        
        this.running.push(promise);
        
        promise.finally(() => {
            this.running = this.running.filter(p => p !== promise);
            this.process();
        });
    }
}

// 使用打印队列
const printQueue = new PrintQueue(2); // 最多同时2个打印任务

// 添加打印任务
const files = ['file1.pdf', 'file2.pdf', 'file3.pdf'];
for (const file of files) {
    printQueue.add(() => printPdf({ path: file, printer: 'Default' }));
}
```

### 内存管理

- **避免在内存中保存大量HTML内容**
- **及时清理打印任务引用**
- **使用流式处理大文件**
- **定期检查和清理打印队列**

import { invoke } from '@tauri-apps/api/core';

async function ping(value) {
