class PosCustomer(models.Model):
    """Walk-in customer registered at POS for loyalty tracking."""
    TIER_CHOICES = [
        ('Bronze', 'Bronze'),
        ('Silver', 'Silver'),
        ('Gold', 'Gold'),
        ('Platinum', 'Platinum'),
    ]

    id = models.UUIDField(primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4, editable=False)
    # Optionally linked to an existing FreshOn user
    user = models.OneToOneField(
        settings.AUTH_USER_MODEL,
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='pos_customer',
    )
    name = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    phone = models.CharField(max_length=15, unique=True)
    email = models.EmailField(blank=True)
    tier = models.CharField(max_length=20, choices=TIER_CHOICES, default='Bronze')
    points = models.PositiveIntegerField(default=0)
    is_pride = models.BooleanField(default=False, help_text="Whether customer is a PRIDE partner")
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
    updated_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now=True)

    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.name} ({self.phone}) — {self.tier}"

    class Meta:
        ordering = ['name']
        verbose_name = "POS Customer"
        verbose_name_plural = "POS Customers"

```python
phone = request.query_params.get('phone', '').strip()
if phone:
    customer = PosCustomer.objects.filter(phone=phone).first()
    if not customer:
        return Response({'error': 'Customer not found'}, status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND)
    txns = PosTransaction.objects.filter(
        customer=customer, transaction_type='SALE'
    ).prefetch_related('items', 'tenders').order_by('-created_at')[:5]
    serializer = PosTransactionSerializer(txns, many=True)
    data = serializer.data
    # Add transaction_type to each
    for item, txn in zip(data, txns):
        item['transaction_type'] = txn.transaction_type
        item['customer_name'] = txn.customer.name if txn.customer else ''
    return Response(data)
```

```python
def get_wallet_balance(self, obj):

    return 0.0
```

class PosTransaction(models.Model):
    """A completed point-of-sale transaction (sale or return)."""
    TRANSACTION_TYPES = [
        ('SALE', 'Sale'),
        ('RETURN', 'Return'),
    ]

    PAYMENT_METHODS = [
        ('Cash', 'Cash'),
        ('UPI', 'UPI'),
        ('Card', 'Card'),
        ('Sodexo', 'Sodexo'),
        ('Split', 'Split Payment'),
    ]

    RECEIPT_CHOICES = [
        ('Print', 'Print'),
        ('WhatsApp', 'WhatsApp'),
        ('SMS', 'SMS'),
    ]

    id = models.UUIDField(primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4, editable=False)
    shift = models.ForeignKey(
        PosShift,
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name='transactions',
    )
    customer = models.ForeignKey(
        PosCustomer,
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
--
class PosTransactionItem(models.Model):
    """Individual product line item within a POS transaction."""
    transaction = models.ForeignKey(
        PosTransaction,
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name='items',
    )
    # Snapshot fields (denormalized for receipt permanence)
    pid = models.CharField(max_length=50, help_text="Product ID from inventory")
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    unit_price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    weighed = models.BooleanField(default=False)
    quantity = models.DecimalField(max_digits=8, decimal_places=3, help_text="Supports fractional for weighed items")
    member_eligible = models.BooleanField(default=False)

    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.quantity}x {self.name} @ ₹{self.unit_price}"

    class Meta:
        ordering = ['name']


class PosTender(models.Model):

        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name='tenders',
    )
    method = models.CharField(max_length=20, choices=PosTransaction.PAYMENT_METHODS)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)

class PosTransaction(models.Model):
    """A completed point-of-sale transaction (sale or return)."""
    TRANSACTION_TYPES = [
        ('SALE', 'Sale'),
        ('RETURN', 'Return'),
    ]

    PAYMENT_METHODS = [
        ('Cash', 'Cash'),
        ('UPI', 'UPI'),
        ('Card', 'Card'),
        ('Sodexo', 'Sodexo'),
        ('Split', 'Split Payment'),
    ]

    RECEIPT_CHOICES = [
        ('Print', 'Print'),
        ('WhatsApp', 'WhatsApp'),
        ('SMS', 'SMS'),
    ]

    id = models.UUIDField(primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4, editable=False)
    shift = models.ForeignKey(
        PosShift,
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name='transactions',
    )
    customer = models.ForeignKey(
        PosCustomer,
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='transactions',
    )
    transaction_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=10, choices=TRANSACTION_TYPES, default='SALE',
    )
    related_transaction = models.ForeignKey(
        'self',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='returns',
        help_text='For RETURN type: links to the original SALE transaction',
    )
    method = models.CharField(max_length=20, choices=PAYMENT_METHODS, default='Cash')
    subtotal = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    member_discount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, default=0)
    surcharge = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, default=0)
    total = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    receipt_delivery = models.CharField(max_length=20, choices=RECEIPT_CHOICES, blank=True)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)

    def __str__(self):
        return f"POS Txn {self.id} — ₹{self.total} ({self.method})"

    class Meta:
        ordering = ['-created_at']


class PosTransactionItem(models.Model):
    """Individual product line item within a POS transaction."""
    transaction = models.ForeignKey(
        PosTransaction,
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,

For `open_cash_drawer`, I need to use `winapi`. Let me write the Rust code:

```rust
#[cfg(windows)]
use winapi::um::winspool::{
    OpenPrinterW, StartDocPrinterW, StartPagePrinter, WritePrinter,
    EndPagePrinter, EndDocPrinter, ClosePrinter, DOC_INFO_1W,
};
#[cfg(windows)]
use winapi::shared::minwindef::{DWORD, LPBYTE, LPDWORD};
#[cfg(windows)]
use std::ffi::OsStr;
#[cfg(windows)]
use std::os::windows::ffi::OsStrExt;

#[cfg(windows)]
fn send_raw_to_default_printer(data: &[u8]) -> Result<(), String> {
    unsafe {
        let mut printer_handle: winapi::um::winnt::HANDLE = std::ptr::null_mut();
        let printer_name: Vec<u16> = OsStr::new("").encode_wide().chain(Some(0)).collect();
        
        if OpenPrinterW(printer_name.as_ptr() as *mut _, &mut printer_handle, std::ptr::null_mut()) == 0 {
            return Err("Failed to open default printer".to_string());
        }

        let doc_name: Vec<u16> = OsStr::new("Cash Drawer").encode_wide().chain(Some(0)).collect();
        let data_type: Vec<u16> = OsStr::new("RAW").encode_wide().chain(Some(0)).collect();
        
        let doc_info = DOC_INFO_1W {
            pDocName: doc_name.as_ptr() as *mut _,
            pOutputFile: std::ptr::null_mut(),
            pDatatype: data_type.as_ptr() as *mut _,
        };

        if StartDocPrinterW(printer_handle, 1, &doc_info as *const _ as *mut _) == 0 {
            ClosePrinter(printer_handle);
            return Err("Failed to start doc".to_string());
        }

        if StartPagePrinter(printer_handle) == 0 {
            EndDocPrinter(printer_handle);
            ClosePrinter(printer_handle);
            return Err("Failed to start page".to_string());
        }

        let mut written: DWORD = 0;
        let data_len = data.len() as DWORD;
        if WritePrinter(printer_handle, data.as_ptr() as *mut _, data_len, &mut written) == 0 {
            EndPagePrinter(printer_handle);
            EndDocPrinter(printer_handle);
            ClosePrinter(printer_handle);
            return Err("Failed to write to printer".to_string());
        }

        EndPagePrinter(printer_handle);
        EndDocPrinter(printer_handle);
        ClosePrinter(printer_handle);
        Ok(())
    }
}
```

Wait, `OpenPrinterW` takes a `LPWSTR` (mutable pointer) for the printer name. Let me check the signature.

Actually, `OpenPrinterW` signature is:
```c
BOOL OpenPrinterW(
  [in]  LPWSTR             pPrinterName,
  [out] LPHANDLE           phPrinter,
  [in]  LPPRINTER_DEFAULTSW pDefault
);
```

In winapi Rust:
```rust
pub unsafe extern "system" fn OpenPrinterW(
    pPrinterName: LPWSTR,
    phPrinter: *mut HANDLE,
    pDefault: *mut PRINTER_DEFAULTSW
) -> BOOL;
```

`LPWSTR` is `*mut WCHAR`, but the function doesn't modify the name, so passing a `*mut _` is fine.

But wait, the `printer_name` needs to be mutable because `OpenPrinterW` expects `LPWSTR` which is `*mut u16`. In practice it won't mutate it.

Also, for the default printer, I should pass an empty string or get the default printer name. Let me get the default printer name properly.

Actually, looking at the Windows API, to get the default printer:
```c
DWORD GetDefaultPrinterW(LPWSTR pszBuffer, LPDWORD pcchBuffer);
```

This is in `winspool`. Let me use it.

```rust
#[cfg(windows)]
use winapi::um::winspool::GetDefaultPrinterW;

#[cfg(windows)]
fn get_default_printer_name() -> Result<String, String> {
    unsafe {
        let mut size: DWORD = 0;
        GetDefaultPrinterW(std::ptr::null_mut(), &mut size);
        if size == 0 {
            return Err("No default printer".to_string());
        }
        let mut buffer: Vec<u16> = vec![0; size as usize];
        if GetDefaultPrinterW(buffer.as_mut_ptr(), &mut size) == 0 {
            return Err("Failed to get default printer name".to_string());
        }
        let len = buffer.iter().position(|&c| c == 0).unwrap_or(buffer.len());
        Ok(String::from_utf16_lossy(&buffer[..len]))
    }
}
```

Then in `send_raw_to_printer`:
```rust
#[cfg(windows)]
fn send_raw_to_printer(printer_name: &str, data: &[u8]) -> Result<(), String> {
    unsafe {
        let name_wide: Vec<u16> = OsStr::new(printer_name).encode_wide().chain(Some(0)).collect();
        let mut printer_handle: winapi::um::winnt::HANDLE = std::ptr::null_mut();
        
        if OpenPrinterW(name_wide.as_ptr() as *mut _, &mut printer_handle, std::ptr::null_mut()) == 0 {
            return Err(format!("Failed to open printer: {}", printer_name));
        }
        ...
    }
}
```

And `open_cash_drawer`:
```rust
#[tauri::command]
fn open_cash_drawer() -> Result<(), String> {
    #[cfg(windows)]
    {
        let printer_name = get_default_printer_name()?;
        let bytes: Vec<u8> = vec![27, 112, 0, 25, 250];
        send_raw_to_printer(&printer_name, &bytes)
    }
    #[cfg(not(windows))]
    {
        println!("Opening cash drawer (non-Windows)...");
        Ok(())
    }
}
```

    11	#[cfg(windows)]
    12	fn get_default_printer_name() -> Result<String, String> {
    13	    unsafe {
    14	        let mut size: DWORD = 0;
    15	        GetDefaultPrinterW(std::ptr::null_mut(), &mut size);
    16	        if size == 0 {
    17	            return Err("No default printer configured".to_string());
    18	        }
    19	        let mut buf: Vec<u16> = vec![0; size as usize];
    20	        if GetDefaultPrinterW(buf.as_mut_ptr(), &mut size) == 0 {
    21	            return Err("Failed to get default printer name".to_string());
    22	        }
    23	        let len = buf.iter().position(|&c| c == 0).unwrap_or(buf.len());
    24	        Ok(String::from_utf16_lossy(&buf[..len]))
    25	    }
    26	}
    27	
    28	#[cfg(windows)]
    29	fn send_raw_to_printer(printer_name: &str, data: &[u8]) -> Result<(), String> {
    30	    use std::ffi::OsStr;
    31	    use std::os::windows::ffi::OsStrExt;
    32	
    33	    unsafe {
    34	        let name_wide: Vec<u16> = OsStr::new(printer_name).encode_wide().chain(Some(0)).collect();
    35	        let mut hprinter: winapi::shared::windef::HANDLE = std::ptr::null_mut();
    36	
    37	        if OpenPrinterW(name_wide.as_ptr() as *mut _, &mut hprinter, std::ptr::null_mut()) == 0 {
    38	            return Err(format!("Failed to open printer: {}", printer_name));
    39	        }
    40	
    41	        let doc_name: Vec<u16> = OsStr::new("POS Command").encode_wide().chain(Some(0)).collect();
    42	        let data_type: Vec<u16> = OsStr::new("RAW").encode_wide().chain(Some(0)).collect();
    43	
    44	        let doc_info = DOC_INFO_1W {
    45	            pDocName: doc_name.as_ptr() as *mut _,
    46	            pOutputFile: std::ptr::null_mut(),
    47	            pDatatype: data_type.as_ptr() as *mut _,
    48	        };
    49	
    50	        if StartDocPrinterW(hprinter, 1, &doc_info as *const _ as *mut _) == 0 {
    51	            ClosePrinter(hprinter);
    52	            return Err("Failed to start print document".to_string());
    53	        }
    54	
    55	        if StartPagePrinter(hprinter) == 0 {
    56	            EndDocPrinter(hprinter);
    57	            ClosePrinter(hprinter);
    58	            return Err("Failed to start print page".to_string());
    59	        }
    60	
    61	        let mut written: DWORD = 0;
    62	        let data_len = data.len() as DWORD;
    63	        if WritePrinter(hprinter, data.as_ptr() as *mut _, data_len, &mut written) == 0 {
    64	            EndPagePrinter(hprinter);
    65	            EndDocPrinter(hprinter);
    66	            ClosePrinter(hprinter);
    67	            return Err("Failed to write to printer".to_string());
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        EndPagePrinter(hprinter);
    71	        EndDocPrinter(hprinter);
    72	        ClosePrinter(hprinter);
    73	        Ok(())
    74	    }
    75	}

---

### 1. Silent Printing (Tenax POS-80)

**`Fpos/package.json`**  
- Replaced incompatible v1 `tauri-plugin-printer` with **Tauri v2-compatible** `tauri-plugin-printer-v2@0.2.4`

**`Fpos/src-tauri/Cargo.toml`**  
- Added `tauri-plugin-printer-v2 = "0.2"` and `winapi` (Windows raw printing)

**`Fpos/src-tauri/src/lib.rs`**  
- Registered plugin: `.plugin(tauri_plugin_printer_v2::init())`
- Added `#[cfg(windows)]` raw-print helpers using `OpenPrinterW` / `WritePrinter` / `ClosePrinter`

**`Fpos/src-tauri/capabilities/default.json`**  
- Added all `printer:` permissions (`allow-print-html`, `allow-get-printers`, etc.)

**`Fpos/src/pos/components/ReceiptModal.tsx`**  
- Added `useRef` to capture receipt DOM
- Imported `printHtml` from `tauri-plugin-printer-v2`
- Replaced `window.print()` with `handlePrint` → calls `printHtml({ html, printer: "Printer POS-80", page_width: 80, page_height: 297 })`
- Falls back to `window.print()` on failure

---

### 2. Phone-based Returns (History Search)

**`backend/apps/pos/models.py`**  
- Added `('Wallet', 'Wallet')` to `PosTransaction.PAYMENT_METHODS`

**`backend/apps/pos/serializers.py`**  
- `PosTenderSerializer`: added `'Wallet'` to choices
- `PosCustomerSerializer`: added `wallet_balance` field (resolves from linked `user.wallet.balance`)

**`backend/apps/pos/views.py`** (`PosOrderLookupView`)  
- Now accepts a `phone` query param → returns the customer's **last 5 SALE transactions**
- Each result includes `transaction_type` and `customer_name`
- Single `receipt_id` lookup unchanged

**`packages/freshon-api/src/modules/pos.ts`**  
- Renamed endpoint to `searchTransactionsByPhone(phone)` → calls `/api/pos/orders/lookup/?phone=...`
- Updated `PosRefundRequest.refund_method` type to include `"Wallet"`

**`Fpos/src/pos/store.ts`**  
- `fetchCustomerTransactions` now calls `pos.searchTransactionsByPhone(phone)`

**`Fpos/src/pos/components/ReturnScreen.tsx`**  
- Already contained the full no-receipt workflow (phone search bar, customer card, Last 5 Transactions table) — fully wired to the new backend endpoint

---

### 3. Wallet Balance Fix

**`Fpos/src/pos/store.ts`** (`pay` action)  
- Already implemented from the prior task: after a successful order, if any tender is `"Wallet"`, the `walletAmt` is subtracted from `selectedCustomer.wallet_balance` in the local state:
  ```ts
  wallet_balance: +((s.selectedCustomer.wallet_balance ?? 0) - walletAmt).toFixed(2)
  ```

---

### 4. Physical Cash Drawer Pulse

**`Fpos/src-tauri/src/lib.rs`** (`open_cash_drawer`)  
- Uses `GetDefaultPrinterW` to resolve the default printer
- Sends the raw ESC/POS drawer-kick sequence `[27, 112, 0, 25, 250]` via `WritePrinter` in RAW mode
- Returns `Err(...)` on Windows printing failure instead of silently succeeding
